maner apperyth thoughe iii fyrſt bokes ſayd iiii bokes haue bē tyme right well deuoutly tranſlated englyſhe famous clerke called mayſter williā atkynſon whiche doctour diuynyte yet moch ſayd tranſlatour ſome cauſe hym mouing ī diuers place lyfte moche parte ſome chapytres ſomtyme varyed fro letter iii chapitre xviii xix chapitre firſte boke alſo dyuers chapitres ſayd iii bokes wyll noble prynce bleſſed memory kyng henry ye vii father vnto ſoueraine lorde kyng nowe kyng henry viii muche trā ſlatyd ſayde noble prynceſſe frenche coulde nat folowe latyn ſo nyghe ne ſo dyrectly ben trā ſlated latyn therfor tranſlated alſo latyn yet neuertheles kepeth ſubſtaūce effect fyrſt trāſlaciō frēche though ſōtyme vary ī wordes reders wyll appere later ende iiii boke ſhorte deuout maner liuynge yf wyll truely illumyned delyueryd blyndnes herte let ſtudy hert therfore frō henſforthe haue meditacion holly fired lyfe holy teachyng ieſu chriſte techynges vertue ghoſtly ſtrength thā techynge al angelles ſayntes throughe grace might haue inner eye ſoule openyd ī ſothfaſte beholdynge goſpelles chriſte ſhulde fynde māna yt ſay ſpiritual fode ſoule oft tymes ſene ſome perſōs ſynnes thā onely knowe diffinicion compūction thou couldeſt byble boke▪ alſo ſeynges phyloſophers herte ſhulde profyte without grace charite al worlde vanyte loue god onely ſerue hym moſte noble moſt excellent wyſdome may creature diſpyſyng worlde drawe dayly nerer nerer kyngdome heuē therfor greate vayne laboure mordinatly wordely ryches ſhortly ſhall peryſhe coueyte honour inordynate pleaſures fleſhely delytes thys lyfe wherby man lyfe ſhal ſore greuouſly punyſhed howe greate vanyte alſo deſyre longe lyfe lytell care good lyfe hide thynges preſent nat prouyde thynges come leue thyngꝭ ſhortely ſhall paſſe awaye nat haſte thyther ioye euerlaſtyng alſo haue thys common prouerbe ofte thy mynde eye nat ſatiſfied ne fully pleaſed ſyght bodely thynge ne eare herynge therfore ſtudye withdrawe loue thy ſoule frō thyngꝭ bene viſyble tourne thynges inuyſyble folowe theyr ſenſualyte hurte theyr owne conſcyence leſe grace god ❧agaynſt vayne ſeculer cōnynge meke knowynge oure ſelfe ii chapytre every man naturally deſyrethe knowe auayle knowledge without dreade god meke huſbandman ſeruethe god acceptable curyouſe phyloſopher whiche conſyderynge courſe heuen wylfully forgetteth hym ſelfe well knoweth hym ſelfe vyle obiecte owne ſyghte hathe delyte vayne prayſynges man knewe thynges worlde without charite ſhulde auayle god iugethe euery man dedes let v therfore c • worlde many thynges knowynge brynge lytell profyte lytell • rute ſoule vnwyſe taketh hede thynge thā ſhal profyte helth ſoule wordꝭ fede nat ſoule hut good lyfe refreſſheth mynde clene conſcyēce bryngeth man ferme ſtable truſte god cōnyng thou haſte thou lyue nat therafter greuouſly ſhalt thou therfore iuged myſuſynge therof therfore ryſe nat thy ſelfe pryde crafte cōnīg gyuē vnto haue therfore feare drede thy herte certayne thou muſte hereafter yelde therfore ſtrayter accompte thou thynke thou knoweſte many thynges haſte great cōnynge yet knowe certayne many mo thyngꝭ thou knoweſt nat ſo thou mayſte nat ryghtwyſely thynke thy ſelfe cōning oughteſt rather confeſſe thyne ygnoraunce vnconnynge wylte thou preferre thy ſelfe connynge ſythe thereby many excellēt connynge thou better lerned lawe thou wylte thyng lerne knowe profytablye helthe thy ſoule lerne vnknowē glade holden vyle noughte vnconnyng thou arte moſte hygh moſte profytable cōnynge man haue ſothfaſte cryme openly yet iuge nat thy ſelfe better thā thou knoweſt nat lōge thou ſhalt perſeuer goodnes al frayle thou ſhalte iuge man frayle thy ſelfe ❧of teachynge trouthe iii chapitre happy bleſſed yf knowe thē hurte v knowe nat therfore greate foly neglygent ſuche thynges profytable neceſſary v labour ſuche thynges curyous dampnable truely yf ſo haue eyen ſe nat auayleth v knowledge kynde werkynge creature truely nothynge whome euerlaſtynge worde ieſus ſpeketh dyſcharged many vayne opynyōs worde thynges procede thynges openly ſhewe crye belyue god man without hym vnderſtandeth trouthe ne ryghtfully iugeth thynges one thynges draweth ī one thynges ſetteth one deſyreth nothynge one may anone ſtablyd ī herte fully pacifyed god trouthe god arte make one perfyte charyte al rede heare myſteries hathe reſceyued aboue lyght vnderſtandynge clene pure ſtable herte nat broken ne lyghtely ouercome ghoſtly laboures doth thynge honoure god clerely mortified hym ſelfe therfore coueyteth fre fro folowynge owne wyl hyndreth thy affeccions nat fully mortyſied wyll ſpirite truely nothyng good deuoute man ſo ordreth outwarde beſynes drawe nat hym loue compell obedient wyll ſpiryte ryght ſet thende perfectyon religyon theſe outwarde obſeruances deuocyō ſhall ſone ended wherfore muſte ſet axe depe rote tree purged paſſyons maye haue quyet mynde wolde euery yere ouercome one vyce ſholde anone come perfectyon feare rather yt contrary wyſe better purer begynnynge oure conuerſyon many yeres conuerted feruour deſyre vertue ſhulde dayly increaſe v encreace age nowe thought great thynge may holde lytell ſpercle feruour fyrſte wolde begynnynge breke euyll inclinacyon haue ſelfe owne wyll ſholde vertuous werkes eaſely greate gladnes herte harde thynge leue euyl cuſtommes herde breke owne wyll▪ moſte herde euermore lye payne endleſly leſe ioyes heuen thou ouercom nat ſmall thyngꝭ lyghte howe ſhalte thou thā ouercome greater reſyſte therfore quykely begynnynge thy euyll inclynacons leue hole thyne euyll cuſtomes leſte haply lytell lytel brynge greater dyffyculte yf thou woldeſt conſydre howe greate inly pea thou ſhulde haue thy ſelfe howe greate gladnes thou ſhuldeſt cauſe behauynge thy ſelfe well ſuppoſe veryly thou woldeſt moche dylygent profyte vertue thou haſte bene thys tyme ❧of profyte aduerſyte xii chapytre good haue ſōtyme gryeffes aduerſites dryue man beholde hym ſelf ſe exyle lerned therby know ought nat put truſte ī worldly thynge good alſo ſuffre ſō tyme cōtradiccyō holden euyll wretched ſynfull thoughe well entend well ſuche thynges helpe v mekenes myghtely defende v frome vayne glory pryde take god better oure iuge wytnes whan outwardely diſpyſed worlde worlde iugeth nat wel v therfor mā ought ſtable ſelf ſo fully ī god aduerſyte ſo euer befall vnto hym ſhal nat nede ſeke outwarde comforte whā good man troubled tempted inquyeted euyll thoughtꝭ thā vnderſtandeth knoweth god moſte neceſſary hym may thyng good without thā ſoroweth waylleth prayethe miſeries ryghtfuly ſuffreth thā yrketh hym alſo wretchydneſſe lyfe coueyteth diſſolued thys bodye dethe chriſte thā alſo ſeeth well maye full peace ne perfyte ſykernes thys worlde ❧of temptacyons reſyſted xiii chapitre longe lyue thys worlde may nat fully without tēptacyon ☞★ iob ſayth temptacyon lyfe man vpon erth therfore euerye man ſhulde well annenſte hys temptacyons watche prayer ghoſtely enemy fynde nat tyme place deceyue hym whiche neuer ſlepethe alwaye goeth • ſekynge whome may deuoute man ſo perfyte ne ſo holye thys worlde ſomtyme ne hathe temptacyons maye nat fully without though tyme verye greuous paynfull yet yf reſyſted profytable mā experyence ſuche temptacyons made meke alſo purged īformed ī diuers maners whiche ſhuld neuer haue knowen experyence ſuche temptacyons bleſſed ſayntes nowe crowned heuen grewe profyted tēptacions tribulacions thoſe coulde nat well bere temptacyons fynally outcome taken perpetuall pryſoners hell order ſo holye ne place ſo ſecrete fully without temptacyon man fully ſyker lyfe corrupte bodye bere mater wherby tēpted inordinate cōcupyſcence wherein borne one temptacyō goth cōmeth ſo deathe better leue ſynne feare deth ♣ dere brother yf thou nat redy daye howe ſhalt thou redy morowe morowe day vncertayne thou canſte nat tell whether thou ſhalte lyue ſo longe profyte v lyue longe whan therby ſo lytell amende oure lyfe longe lyfe dothe nat alwaye brynge v amendemente ofte tymes encreaſethe ſynne wolde god myghte one daye well conuerſaūt thys worlde many rekyne theyr yeres cōuerſyon yet lytell frute amendemēt ne good example ſene theyr conuerſacyon yf ferefull dye peraduenture peryllous lyue long bleſſed perſonns euer haue houre deth theyr eyen euery day diſpoſe thē ſelfe dye yf thou euer ſaueſt man dye remembre thou muſte nedely go ſame waye mornynge doute whether thou ſhalle lyue tyll nyght nyght thynke nat thy ſelfe ſure lyue tyll morowe alway redy liue ſuch maner deth fynde nat vnprouided remēber many haue dyed ſodaynly vnꝓuyded lorde hath called thē ſuche houre leeſt went whan laſte houre ſhall come thou ſhalt beginne fele al otherwyſe thy lyfe paſſed faythfull ſoule prepayre thy herte chryſte thy ſpouſe may come well ye ſaith ſelfe ſo loueth ſhall kepe cōmaundemēt father holy ghoſte ſhall come hym ſhall make hym dwellynge place gyue therfore chryſte fre entre thy herte kepe al thynges letteth entre whē thou art ryche ynough oonly ſhall ſuffice ſhall thy prouyder defender thy faythfull helper euery neceſſyte ſo thou ſhalte nat nede put thy truſte without hym man ſoone chaungyd lyghtly fallyth awaye chryſte abydeth euer ſtandeth ſtrongly louer ende greate truſte put man mortall frayle thoughe ryght moche profytable alſo muche belouyd vnto ne greate heuynes taken though ſomtyme turne againſt daye tomorowe maye happen agaynſte maye ofte turne dothe wynde put thy full truſte therfor ī god let thy loue drede aboue thynges wyll anſwere wyll al thynges ſhalbe moſt nedefull moſte expediente thou haſte place longe abydyng ſo euer thou become thou arte ſtraunger pylgryme neuer ſhalte thou fynde parfeyte reſte tyll thou fully oned god doſte thou loke haue reſte ſyth nat thy reſtyng place thy ful reſte muſte heuē ly thynges erthely thynges thou muſte beholde thinges tranſitory ſhortly paſſynge awaye wel ware thou cleue nat ouer moche leſte thou taken loue theym ende periſſhe therby let thy thought alwaye vpwarde god dyrecte thy prayer chriſte contynually thou may nat frailte thy ſelfe alwaye occupye thy mynde contemplacion godhede occupyed mynde hys paſſyon hys bleſſed woundes make dwellynge place yf thou fle deuoutely wounde chriſtes ſyde markes paſſyon thou ſhalte fele greate cōforte euery trouble ſhalte lytell force thoughe thou openly diſpyſed worlde euyll wordꝭ ſo euer ſpoken ſhal lytel greue maiſter chriſte dyſpyſed worlde men moſte nede forſaken acquayntaunce frendes lefte amonge ſhames rebuke wolde ſuffre wronges benought ſet worlde wyll nat perſone doo v wronge ne diſprayſe oure dedes chriſte many aduerſaries backebytours wolde haue oure frendes louers howe ſh • lde thy pacience maketh man perfytely dyſpyſe hym ſelfe true inwarde loue god fre inordinate affeccions may anone tourne hym ſelf frely god lyfte hym ſelfe vp ſpirite contē placion frutefully reſte hym chriſte alſo whome thinges eſtemed nat taken thought worldly people wyſe rather taught god thā mā īwardly lyfte minde vpwardly god lytell regarde outwarde thīges nedeth nat ſeke time place go prayer doo good dedes vertuous occupaciōs ghoſtly mā may ſone gather ſelf together fyxe mynde god neuer ſuffereth fully occupyed outwarde thynges therfore outwarde laboures worldely occupacions neceſſary tyme worldly thīg thā ſhuld beloued ſo moche hys mynde hyndred letted true ordynate loue ſhulde haue god thou well purged inordinate affectyons thane ſo euer ſhulde befall ſhulde tourne thy ghoſtely muche defouleth ſoule vnclene loue creature yf thou forſake comforted worldly thynges outwardly thou mayſte beholde parfytely heuenly thynges thou ſhalte ſynge contynually laudes prayſynges hym greate giue eate tre lyfe ♣ heuēly cōforte ſomtyme gyuē mā may ſtronge ſuffre aduerſyties foloweth temptacyō nat lyfte vp ī pryde thynke worthy ſuche conſolacyon ghoſtely enemy ſlepeth nat ne fleſhe nat yet fully mortifyed therfore thou ſhalt neuer ceſſe prepayre thy ſelfe ghoſtely batayle thou haſte enemyes euery ſide euer wyl redy aſſayle let thy good purpoſe ❧of yeldynge thankes god hys manyfolde grace x chapitre ſekeſt thou reſt ſyth thou arte borne laboure diſpoſe thy ſelf pacyence rather thā confortes bere croſſe penaunce rather haue gladnes temporall man wolde nat gladly haue ſpirituall cōfortes yf myght alway kepe thē ſpirytuall cōfortes excede far worldely delytes bodely pleaſures al worldly delytes eyther foule vayne ghoſtely delytes onely iocunde honeſte brought forthe vertues ſent god clene ſoule ſuche confortes man may haue whan wolde tyme tētacyon tarieth nat lōge falſe lybertye wyll ouermoche truſte haue ſelfe moche contrary heuenly viſitacyons lorde dothe well ſendynge ſuche confortes nat well whā yelde na • thankes therfore againe greateſt cauſe giftes grace maye nat lyghtly come v vnkynde giuer yelde nat thākes hym goodnes cōmeth grace alwaye gyuen theym redy yelde thankes therfore agayne therfore ſhal taken proude man wrute gyuen meke man wolde none conſolacyō ſhuld take compunction ne wolde none contemplacyon ſhulde lyfte ſoule preſumpcion euery hyghe thyng ſyght man nat holy ne euery deſyre nat cleane pure ne euery ſwete thing nat good ne lefe dere man nat alway pleſaūt god ſhall therfore gladly take ſuche gyftꝭ wherby ſhalbe redy forſake ſelfe owne wyll knoweth cōfortes come gyfte grace knoweth alſo howe ſharpe paynfull abſentynge grace ſhall nat dare thynke goodnes commeth hym felfe ſhall openly confeſſe hym ſel • e ryght pore naked vertue yelde therfore god thy ſelfe thyne ſaye thāke god manyfolde grace blame thy ſelfe thy offence holde alway ſure grounde ſure foundacyon mekenes thā highnes vertue ſhall ſhortely giuen vnto hyghe tourne vertue maye nat longe ſtande borne vp lowe foundacyon mekenes moſte greate heuen leſte theyr owne ſyght gloryous meker ſelfe ful truthe heuenly ioye nat deſyrous vayne glory prayſinge man alſo groūdely ſtabled confirmed god maye wyſe lyft vp pryde aſcribe al goodnes god ſeke glorye ne vayne prayſynges worlde deſyre onely ioy glorified god deſyre ī herte may honoured lauded prayſed aboue al thynges ī hym ſelfe ſayntes alwaye thynge perfyte men moſte coueyte moſte deſyre brynge aboute thou louynge thankefull god leſte benefyte gyueth thā thou ſhalte apte withdrawen praye deuoutely maye ſhortely come agayne thā meke lowe ſpirite leſe nat agayne preſumpcyon pryde herte ❧of ſmale nombre louers croſſe xi chapytre ieſus hathe many louers kyngdome heuen hath fewe berers hys croſſe many deſyre hys conſolacyon fewe deſyre tribulacion fyndeth many felowes eatynge drynking fyndeth fewe abſtynēce faſtynge mē wolde ioye chriſte fewe wyll thynge ſuffre • longe aduerſyte foloweth prayſe hym bleſſe hym whan receyue benyfayte hī ieſu lytell withdrawe hym lytell forſaketh anone fall ſom great grudgynge ouer greate deieccyon open deſperacyon loue ieſu purely hym ſelfe nat theyr owne profyte commodyte bleſſe hym hartely temptacyon tribulaciō aduerſytes tyme conſolacyon neuer ſent conſolacyon yet wolde alway laude hym prayſe hym ☞ howe maye loue ieſu helpe ſoule yf pure cleane nat myxte īordinate loue hym ſelfe truely nothynge maye nat euer loke worldly confortes worldly conſolacyons called worldly marchauntes worldely louers rather louers god nat openly ſhewe theyr dedes rather loue ſelfe god yes truely ♣ may foundē wyl ſerue god frely purely without lokinge ſome rewarde agayne maye founde ſo ſpyrituall clerely deliuered byrafte loue hym ſelfe truely poore ſpiryte holy auoyded loue creaturꝭ trowe none ſuche foūd far hen far countreys man gyue hys ſubſtance god yet nought great penaunce ſynnes yet lytell yf haue greate connynge kepe thynge hym ſelfe pryuate loue whan hath done ought fele hym ſelfe nothynge done ne thynke nat greate ſome myght thinke great thynke hym ſelfe truely vnprofytable ſeruaūt ☞ auctoure trouth ſauioure cryſt ſayth whā ye haue done cōmaundyd yet ſaye ye vnprofytable ſeruauntes thā thus may wel called pore ſpyryte naked priuate loue may wel ſay prophete dauyd ☞ onede god pore meke herte ſhalte go lyfe euerlaſtynge hath gone berynge croſſe dyed vpō croſſe thou ſhuldeſt lyke wyſe beare hym croſſe penaunce tribulaciō thou ſhuldeſte redy lyke wyſe loue ſuffre deth nede requyre hath done thou dye hym thou ſhalte lyue hym yf thou felowe hym payne thou ſhalte hym glory beholde thā howe croſſe ſtandeth howe dyeng worlde lyeth helth waye lyfe true inwarde peace waye croſſe daily mortifiyng body ſpiryte go whether thou wylte ſeke lyſt thou ſhalt neuer finde aboute ne byneth within ne without hygh excellente ne ſure way chriſte thā way holy croſſe dyſpoſe euery thyng thy wyll thou ſhalt neuer fynde thou muſt neceſſyte ſōwhat ſuffre eyther thy wyll agaynſt thy wyll ſo thou ſhalte alway fynde croſſe eyther thou ſhalt fele payne ī thy body thy ſoule thou ſhalte haue troube ſpirite thou ſhalte ſomtyme thou forſaken god somtyme thou ſhalt vexed thy neyghboure yet paynfull thou ſhalt ſomtyme greuous thy ſelfe thou ſhalt fynde meane delyuered behoueth ſuffre tyll ſhall pleaſe almyghty god hys goodnes otherwyſe dyſpoſe wyll yt thou ſhalte lerne ſuffre trybulacyon without conſolacyō thou mayſt therby lerne holly ſubmyt thy ſelfe hym tribulacyō made meek thou fyrſte man feleth paſſyon chryſte ſo effectuouſly feleth lyke payne chryſte dyd croſſe alway redy euery abydeth thou mayſte nat fle ne fully eſcape euer thou become ſo euer thou become thou ſhalt bere thy ſelfe aboute ye ſo thou ſhalte alwaye fynde thy ſelfe tourne thou wylte beneth within without thou ſhalte fynde croſſe euery ſyde ſo ſhalbe neceſſary thou alwaye kepe pacyence behoueth yf thou wylte haue warde peace deſerue perpetuall crowne heuen yf thou wylte gladely bere croſſe ſhall bere ſhal brynge ende thou deſyreſt thou ſhalte neuer haue thinge ſuffre yf thou bere thys croſte agaynſte thy wyll thou makeſte greate burden thy ſelfe wyll greuous yet behoueth bere happen pul awaye one croſſe ſaye one trybulacyon yet ſurely wyll come happely greuous thā fyrſte • oweſte thou eſcape neuer yet mortall mā myght eſcape ſaynte thys worlde hath ben without thys croſſe without ſome trouble truly lorde ieſu nat one houre without ſome ſorowe payne long lyued behoueth hym ſuffre death ryſe agayne ſo entre glory howe thou ſekeſte way heuen playne hygh waye croſſe lyfe chriſte croſſe marterdome thou ſekeſt pleaſure ioye thou erreſte greatly yf thou ſeke thynge ſuffre thys mortall lyfe thus vexed payne nat ſef • e hooly without conforte ſeethe well greate frute hygh rewarde ſhall growe vnto hym berynge croſſe whan man frely ſubmitteth hym ſelfe vnto ſuche trybulacyon burden trybulacyon ſodeynly tourned great truſte heuenly cōſolaciō fleſſhe punyſſhed trybulacion ſoule ſtrengthed dayly inwarde conſolacion ſomtyme ſoule ſhall fele ſuche cōforte aduerſyties loue deſyre hath conformed chryſte crucified wolbe nat without ſorowe trouble conſydereth wel may ſuffre loue acceptable ſhall hym lyfe come workyng nat power man grace god ſay frayle man ſhulde take loue bodely kynde ſo muche abhorreth fleeth nat power mā gladly bere croſſe loue croſſe chaſtyce body make burn wyll ſpyrite • e honoures gladly ſuſtayne reprefes diſpyſe hym ſelfe coueyt diſpyſed pacyently ſuffre aduerſyties dyſpleaſures therof nat deſyre maner profite worlde yf thou truſte thy ſelfe thou ſhalt neuer bryng mater aboute yf thou truſte god ſhall ſende ſtrength heuen worlde fleſhe ſhalbe made ſubiecte yea thou ſtrongly armed fayth merked croſſe chryſte houſholde ſeruaūte thou ſhalt nat nede fere ghoſtly enemy ſhal alſo made ſubiecte ſo ſhall haue power agaynſte purpoſe thy ſelfe therfore true faythfull ſeruaūte god bere māfully croſſe thy lorde ieſu thy loue crucyfied vpon croſſe prepayre thy ſelfe ſuffre maner aduerſytes dyſcomodites thys wretched lyfe ſo ſhall ſo euer thou hyde remedye eſcape thou muſte kepe thy ſelfe alway pacyēce thou deſyre dere welbeloued frende chryſte drynke affectuouſly hym draught chalyce trybulacyon conſolacyons cōmitte wyl order knoweth lyfe ❧howe ought conuerſaunte god trouth mekenes v chapitre mi ſone ſayth lorde ieſu walke trouthe mekenes ſeke alwaye ſymplenes playnnes herte walketh trouthe ſhalbe defended perylles daungers trouthe ſhall delyuer hym fro deceyuours al euyl ſaynges wycked people trouth delyuer thou arte fre thou ſhalte lytell care vayne ſayinges people ♣ lorde true thou ſayeſte done thy ſayng beſech thy trouth may teache kepe fynally leade bleſſed endynge may delyuer euyll affeccyons inordynate loue maye walke fredome ſpyrite lybertye herte trouth ſayth agayne ſhal teache acceptable likyng thinke thy ſynnes paſt great diſpleaſure ſorowe herte neuer thynke thy ſelfe worthy called holy vertuous good dedes thou haſte done thou thynke howe greate ſynner thou arte belapped boundē many folde ſynnes paſſions thy ſelfe thou droweſte nought ſone falleſte ſone arte ouercome ſone troubeled ſone arte thou brokē laboure payne thou haſt nothyng wherof thou mayſt ryghtwyſely glorify thy ſelfe many thingꝭ thou haſte wherfore thou oughteſt diſpiſe thy ſelfe thou arte vnſtable weyke ghoſtly werkes thou knoweſte mayſte thynke let nothynge therfore ſeme greate nothyng precyous nothyng worthy reputacion ne worthy prayſed thy ſyght euerlaſtynge let euerlaſtynge trouth moſte lykyng mooſte pleaſaunte aboue thynges thyne owne ſynne vylete moſte myſlykynge moſte dyſpleaſaunte dreade nothynge ſo muche ne reproue nothynge ſo muche ne let nothynge ſo muche hated ne fle thou nothynge ſo muche thy ſynnes wyckednes ſhulde diſpleaſe thā ſhulde loſſe al worldly thynges ☞★ walke nat purelye throughe pryde curioſyte thē ſelfe deſyre ſerch knowe hygh thynges godhede forgettyng ſelfe helthe theyr owne ſoules suche perſones fall ofte tymes greate temptacyons greuous ſynnes theyr pryde curioſyte whiche tourned agaynſte leue ſelfe withoute helpe counſeyle ☞ drede therfore iugemente god wrathe hym almighty diſcuſſe nat ne ſerche nat ſecretes ſerche well thyne owne iniquity howe ofte howe greuouſly thou haſte offendyd hym howe many good dedes thou haſte neglygantly omytted lefte vndone whiche thou myghteſt well haue done perſons bere theyr deuocion bokꝭ ſome ymages ſome outwarde tokenes figure ſome haue theyr mouthe lytell theyr harte ſome ther • hath theyr reaſon clerely illumyned lyght true vnderſtandynge wherby theyr affeccyon ſo purged purifyed frō loue erthely thynges may alway coueyte deſyre heuē ly thyngꝭ ſo muche greuous theym erthely thynges thē alſo ryght greate payne ſerue neceſſytes bodye thynke al time loſte go aboute suche perſones fele knowe well ſpirite trouth ſpeketh theyr ſoules teacheth diſpyſe erthly thynges loue heuenly thynges forſake worlde tranſitory deſyre day nyght come thether ioye euer laſtynge whiche brynge v lorde ieſus amen ❧of meruaylous effecte loue god vi chapytre bleſſed thou heuenly father father lorde ieſu chryſte thou haſte vouchedſafe remēbre thy pooreſt ſeruaunte ſomtyme doſte comforte thy gra • yous preſence vnworthye comforte bleſſe glorifye alwaye onely begotten ſone holy ghoſte without endyng amen ♣o lorde god moſte faythfull louer whan thou cōmeſt herte inwarde partyes ioye thou arte glory ioye herte hope hole refuge trouble aſmuch yet feble loue vnperfyte vertue therfore haue nede haue conforte helpe voutcheſafe therfore ofte tymes vyſyte inſtructe thy holy teachynger delyuer fro euyll paſſyons helpe ſyke herte al inordinate affeccyons maye inwardely healed purged inordinate affeccions vyces made apte able loue ſtronge ſuffre ſtable perſeuer loue greate thynge good onely maketh heuy bourden lyght bereth lyke balaunce thingꝭ pleaſaunte diſpleaſaunte bereth heuy bourdē feleth nat maketh bytter thyngꝭ ſauoury ſwete alſo noble loue ieſu perfytly prynted mannes ſoule maketh man great thynges ſtyreth hym alwaye deſyre perfeccyon growe grace goodnes loue wyll alway haue hys mynde vpwarde god wyll nat occupyed loue worlde loue well alſo fre worldly affeccyons inwarde ſyght ſoule nat darked ne let ne affeccyon heuenly thynges nat put fre liberte inordinate wynning leſynge worldly thynges nothynge therfore ſweter loue nothynge hygher nothynge ſtronger nothynge larger nothynge ioyfuller nothynge fuller ne nothynge better heuen ne erthe loue diſcendeth frō god may nat reſte finally nothing lower god ♣ suche louer fleethe hyghe renneth ſweftely mery god fre ſoule gyueth hath reſtethe one hygh goodnes aboue thynges whome goodnes floweth procedeth beholdeth nat onely gyfte gyuer aboue gyfte loue knoweth meaſure feruent without meaſure▪ feleth burden regardeth laboure deſyreth may attayne cōplaineth none inpoſſibilyte thynketh thynge maye done beloued poſſyble lawful vnto hym loue therfore dothe many great thynges bryngeth effecte wherin louer faynteth fayleth koue waketh muche fle yet lytell ſlepyng ſlepeth nat faynteth nat wery reſtrayned lyberte greate fredome ſeeth cauſes frre fereth nat quycke bronde ſparkle fyre flameth alway vpwarde feruoure loue god ſpeciall helpe grace delyuered frō perylles daungers thus ghoſtely louer knoweth well thys voyce meaneth whiche ſayth thus ☞ thou lorde god art hole loue deſyre thou arte myne thyne sprede thou herte thy loue may taſte fele howe ſwete ſerue howe ioyfull laude molten thy loue bounden loue go far aboue ſelfe greate wonder feruoure fele thy vnſpekable goodnes ſhall ſynge ſonge loue ſhall folowe beloued hyghnes thought ſo euer thou go ſoule ſhal neuer wery praiſe ioyfull ſong ghoſtely loue ſhall ſynge ſhall loue ſelfe nat ſelfe lawe loue commaundeth whiche • giuē loue ſwyfte pure meke ioyous glad ſtronge pacyent faythfull wyſe forberynge manly neuer ſekynge hym ſelfe ne hys owne wyll whan ſo euer man ſeketh hym ſelfe falleth fro loue alſo loue circumſpecte meke ryghtwyſe nat tender nat lyght ne hedyng vayne thynges ſober chaſte ſtable quyet well ſtabled hys outwarde wyttes loue ſubiecte obedyent hys prelate vyle diſpiſable hys owne ſyght deuout thankefull god truſtynge alway hopyng hym whan hath lytell deuocyō lytell ſauoure hym withoute ſome ſorowe payne man may lyue loue nat alwaye redye ſuſſre ſtande fully wyll hys beloued nat worthy called louer behoueth louer ſuffre gladly harde bytter thyngꝭ hys beloued nat declyne hys loue contrarious thynge may befall vnto hym ❧of proufe true louer god vii chapytre mi ſon ſayth ſauyour chriſte thou arte nat yet ſtronge wyſe louer lytel aduerſite thou leueſt anone thou haſte begonne ſeruice great deſyre thou ſekeſt outwarde cōſolacyons ſtronge faythfull louer god ſtandeth ſtable aduerſytes gyueth lytell hed • deceytfull perſuacyons enemye pleaſe hym proſperyte ſo dyſpleaſe hym nat aduerſyte wyſe louer conſydereth nat ſo muche gyfte hys louer doth loue gyuer regardethe loue gyfte accompteth gyftes lytell comparyſon beloued giueth thē noble louer reſtethe nat gyfte aboue gyftes ferthermore nat loſte thoughe thou ſomtyme fele leſſe deuocyō ſaintes thou woldeſte ſyde ſwete ghoſtely deſyre thou feleſt ſomtyme thy lorde ieſu feable gyfte grace gyuen thy conforte lyfe taſte heuenly glory lyfe come nat good thou leue ouermoche ſuche confortes lyghtely come go wyll gyuer ſtryue alway without ceſſyng agaynſte euyl mocyons ſyne dyſpyſe ſuggeſtyons enemye token perfyte loue greate meryte ſyneguler grace let vanitis ne ſtraunge fantyſyes trouble matter ſo euer be▪ kepe thyne intente thy purpoſe alwaye hole ſtronge thynke nat illuſion thou arte ſodeynly rauyſſhed exceſſe mynde thou arte ſone tourned agayne thy fyrſte lyghtnes herte thou ſuffereſt ſuche lyghtnes rather agaynſte thy wyll thy wyll therfore thou dyſpleaſed therwith ſhalbe greate meryte perdicion ☞ knowe ſayth ou • lorde olde auncyente enemye fynde wyll aſſaye lette thy good wyll extincte good deſyre thou haſte goodnes wyll alſo hyndre good warkes deuoute exerciſes maye ſay honoure worſhype thou arte bounden gyue ſayntes mynde paſſyon remembraunce thyne owne ſynnes frō diligente kepynge thy herte good meditacyons ſtedfaſte purpoſe profyte vertue wyll alſo put thy minde many ydell thoughtꝭ make • yrke ſone wery prayer redynge good vertuous warkes meke cōfeſſyon dyſpleaſeth hym muche wyl let man ſhall nat howſyled beleue hym nat ne care nat hym thoughe aſſayle neuer ſo muche make malice retourne ſelfe agayne ſay thus ❧ go frō thou wycked ſpiryte thou aſhamed thou arte foule vggely woldeſt brynge ſuche thynges mynde go fro thou falſe deceyuer mākynde thou ſhalt haue parte ſauyoure ieſu ſtandeth myghty warryour ſtronge champyō thou ſhalt fle away thy confuſyon leuer ſuffre moſte cruell deth conſente thy malycious ſtyrrynges ſtyll therfore thou curſed fynde ceſſe thy malyce ſhall neuer aſſente thoughe thou vexe neuer ſo muche lorde lyght helth whome ſhall drede defender lyfe ſhall feare truely thoughe hoſte men aryſe agaynſte herte ſhall nat drede god helper redemer ſayth lorde agayne ſuche ſoule ☞ stryue alwaye true knyght agaynſte ſtyrryngꝭ enemy yf thou ſomtyme thy fraylte ouercome ryſe ſone agayne take ſtrength thā thou haddeſt fyrſte truſte verely haue grace cōforte god thā thou haddeſte beware alwaye vayne glory pryde therby many perſons haue fallē great errours greate blyndnes ſoule ſo far hath ben ryght nyghe incurable therfore great example matter perpetuall mekenes fall ruyne ſuche proude folkes folyſhely haue preſumed ſelfe haue ende finally peryſhed theyr preſumpcyon ❧howe grace kepte cloſe vertue mekenes viii chapytre mi ſonne muche expedyente moche ſuerer waye thou hyde grace deuocyon nat ſpeake moche ne muche regarde rather dyſpiſe thy ſelfe thinke thy ſelfe vnworthy ſuche gracyous gyfte god ſpeke nat good cleaue muche ſuche affection may ſone tourned cō trary whā thou haſt grace deuociō cōſider howe wretched howe nedy thou wert wōt whā thou hadeſt ſuche grace profyte encreaſe lyfe ſpyritual nat whā thou haſt deuociō rather whan thou canſte mekely pacyently bere withdrawynge abſentinge therof yet nat leue thy prayer ne thy good dedes thou arte accuſtomed vndone thy power farre thou doſte thy beſte therin forgetteſt nat thy duety therfore thou arte nat negligente dulnes vnquietnes mynde thou feleſte neuertheles many perſones whan aduerſyte falleth anone vnpacyēt made therby ſlowe dull good dede hyndre ſelfe greatly nat power man way ſhal take onely grace god dyſpoſe wyll ſende cōforte whā wyll muche wyll whome wyll ſhal pleaſe hym none otherwyſe vnware perſones throughe vndeſcrete deſyre haue haue grace deuocyon haue diſtroyed themſelfe wolde doo theyr power wolde nat knowe meſure gyfte ne thy lytelnes owne ſtrength rather wolde folowe pryde theyr herte thā iugement reaſon bycauſe preſumed greater thynges pleaſaunt god therfore loſt anone grace lefte nedy without comforte whiche thought haue buylded theyr neſtes heuen ſo taught nat preſume ſelfe mekely truſte god hys goodnes alſo ſuche perſones begynners yet lacke experyence ghoſtly trauayle may lyghtely erre deceyued wyll ruled counſayle wyll nedely folowe theyr owne coūſayle wyll wyſe remoued fro theyr owne wyll wyll perylous ī ende nat lyghtly ſene wyſe cōnynge theyr owne ſight wyll mekely ruled ordered better haue lytell conninge mekenes great cōnyng vayne lykyng therin better haue lytell connyng grace muche cō nynge wherof thou ſhuldeſte proude alſo doth nat diſcretly tyme deuocion ſetteth ſelfe ſpiritual myrth heuenly gladnes forgetteth former deſolacion meke dreade god ne dothe nat well vertuouſly tyme trouble maner aduerſyte grauite bereth ſelfe ouermuch deſperatly feleth nat ne thynketh nat ſo truſtfully ought tyme peace ghoſtly conforte wyll thynke hym ſelfe ouer muche ſyker cōmō ly tyme batayle temptacyon ſhalbe founde ouermuhe deiecte ferefull thou couldeſt alwaye abyde meke lytell thyne owne ſyght couldeſt order well mocyons thyne owne ſoule thou ſhuldeſt nat ſo ſone fall preſumpcyō dyſpayre ne ſo lyghtly offende almyghtye god wherfore thys good holſome coūſayle whan thou haſte ſpyryte feruoure thou thynke howe thou ſhalt whan feruoure paſſed whan happeneth ſo thou thynke may ſone come agayne whiche honoure thy prouynge haue withdrawen time profitable thou ſhuldeſte ſo proued thou ſhuldeſt alway haue proſperous thynges thy wyll merytes nat thought greate perſone bycauſe hath many vyſyons many ghoſtly cōfortes hath clere vnderſtandyng ſcripture ſet hyghe degre ſtably groūded mekenes fulfylled charyte ſeke hooly worſhyppe god nothinge regardeth hym ſelfe fully ī herte diſpyſe hym ſelfe alſo coueyteth dyſpyſed may haue good truſt hath ſomwhat profyted grace ſhall ende haue greate rewarde god hys good trauayle amen ❧howe ſhall thynke throughe mekenes ſelfe vyle abiecte ſyght god ix chapyter shall lorde ieſu dare ſpeke duſte aſſhes verely thynke ſelfe better aſſhes duſte thou ſtandeſte agaynſte alſo myne owne ſynnes bere wytnes agaynſte maye nat ſaye yf dyſpyſe ſelfe ſet ſelfe noughte thynke ſelfe aſſhes duſte thy grace ſhalbe nyghe vnto lyght true vnderſtandyng ſhall entre herte ſo preſumpcion pryde ſhall drowned vale mekenes throughe parfyte knowynge wretchednes mekenes thou ſhalt ſhewe vnto haue ben fro whens came nought knewe nat yf lefte ſelfe thā naught feblenes inꝑfeccion thou voucheſafe lytell beholde anone made ſtronge fylled newe ioy meruayle wretche ſo ſone lyfte vp fro vnſtablenes beholdynge heuenly thynges ſo louyngly enhalſed ſelfe fall downe alwaye erthely lykynges thy loue lorde cauſeth al preuenth helpeth neceſſytyes kepeth warely perylles daūgers dayly lyke fall haue loſte alſo ſelfe inordynate loue haue ſelfe keping agayne haue founde bothe therfore wyll depely henſeforth ſet ſelfe nought delygently ſeke thā haue done ī tyme paſte thou lorde ieſu thou doſte aboue merytes aboue aſke deſyre bleſſed thou thy warkes thoughe vnworthy good thynges yet thy goodnes neuer ceſſeth well ſo many whiche vnkynde tourned ryght far fro tourne v lorde therfore agayne may henſforwarde louynge thankeful meke deuoute ye thou arte helth thou arte vertue ſtrength body ſoule none thou therfore ioye glory euerlaſtyngly bleſſe heuen amen ❧howe thynges referred god ende euery warke x chapyter mi ſone ſayeth ſauyour chryſte muſte ende thy war • e thou deſyre happy bleſſed thou referre goodnes frō whome goodnes commeth thā ſhall pourged made cleane thyne warde affeccyons whiche el wolde euyll enclyned thy ſelfe creature thou ſeke thy ſelfe thynge ende thy warke anone thou fayleſt thy doyng waxeſt drye bareyn moyſter grace wherfore thou muſte refarre al thyngꝭ gyue beholde therfore thinges flowynge ſpryngynge oute ſouerayne goodnes reduce al thingꝭ theyr original begīninge ſmale great poore ryche quycke ſpringyng well drawe water lyfe ſerueth freely good wyll ſhall receyue grace grace wyll glorifye hym ſelf hym ſelfe wyll fully ioy ī thyng beſyde ſhall nat ſtableſſhed parfyte ioy ne dilated ſoule ſhall letted anguyſſhed many wayes trewe fredome ſpiryte thou ſhalte therfore aſcrybe goodnes thy ſelfe ne thou ſhalte nat thynke perſone hath goodnes hym ſelfe thou yelde alwaye goodnes without whome man hath nothyng haue gyuen wyll haue agayne great ſtraynes wyll loke haue thankynges therfore thys trouthe wherby dryuen away al maner vayne glory pryde herte heuēly grace perfyte charyte enter thy herte ſhall enuye ne vnquyetnes mynde ne pryuate loue haue true ruele charyte god ſhall ouercome thynges ſhall dilate enflame al power thy ſoule wherfore thou vnderſtandeſt ryght thou ſhalte neuer ioy onely thou ſhalte haue truſte man good god alone aboue thynges honoured thynges bleſſed amen ❧that ſwete delectable ſerue god forſake worlde xi chapyter howe ſhall yet ſpeake agayne lorde ieſu nat ceaſe ſhall ſaye • are lorde god kynge heuen ★ howe greate habundaūce ye ſwetnes whiche thou haſt hyde kept drede thē loue theyr herte ſerue verely vnſpekeable ſwetnes cō templacyō thou giueſt loue thys lorde thou haſte moſte ſhewed ſwetnes thy charyte whan nat thou madeſt whan erred far thou broughteſte agayne ſerue thou cō maundeſt alſo ſhal loue the♣ fountayne loue euerlaſtynge ſhall ſay howe may forgette haſte vouchedſafe thus loungly remēbre whan like haue periſhed thou ſhewedeſt thy mercy aboue coulde haue thought deſyred haſte ſente thy grace thy loue aboue merites ſhall gyue agayne thys goodnes nat gyuen men forſake worlde take ſolytary lyfe onely ſerue yet great thynge ſerue whome euerye creature boūden ſerue ought nat therfore ſeme greate thynge ſerue rather ſhulde ſeme meruayle wonder thou wylte voucheſafe receyue ſo poore ſo vnworthy creature thy ſeruyce thou wylt ioyne thy welbeloued ſeruaūtes lo lorde al thingꝭ haue al ſeruyce thyne yet thy goodnes ſuche thou rather ſerueſt lo heuen erthe planettes ſterres theyr cōtentes whiche thou haſte created ſerue man redy thy byddyng dayly thou haſte commaunded thou haſte alſo ordeyned angel myniſtery man aboue thys thou haſte vouchedſafe ſerue man thy ſelfe haſte ꝓmyſed gyue thy ſelfe vnto hym ſhal thā gyue againe thouſāde folde goodnes wolde god myght ſerue dayes lyfe leſte myght one day able faylthful ſeruice thou arte worthy al honour ſeruyce prayſinge euer thou arte lorde god thy pooreſt ſeruaunt moſte boundē al loue prayſe neuer ought wax wery praiſing aſke deſyre ſay may alwaye laude prayſe voutchſafe therfore moſt mercyfull lorde ſupplye wanteth great honoure ſerue al erthly thynges diſpyſe loue ſhall haue great grace frely ſubmytteth ſelfe thy holy ſeruyce ſhal fynde alſo moſte ſwete conſolacyon holy ghooſte ſhall haue great fredome ſpirite forſake al worldly buſynes choſe harde ſtrayte lyfe worlde thy name ♣ fre ioyfull ſeruice god man made fre holy alſo bleſſed ſyght god ♣ holy ſtate religyon whiche maketh man lyke aungelles pleaſaunt god dredfull wycked ſpirites faythful people ryght hyghly cōmendable ſeruice muche enhalſed alway deſired hyghe goodnes wonne euerlaſtyng ioy gladnes gotten withoute ende ❧that deſyres herte ought well examyned well modered xii chapyter mi ſone ſayth lorde behoueth lerne many thynges thou haſte nat yet well lerned lorde thou order thy deſyres thy affeccyons hooly pleaſure thou nat louer thy ſelfe deſyrous folower wyll thynges knowe well deſyres ofte moue thys thynge conſyder well whether thou moued principally honoure thyn owne ī cauſe thou ſhalt wel cōtēted ſo euer • thynge remayne thy hert thyne owne wyll letteth hyndereth beware therfore thou leue nat muche thyne owne deſyre without counſayle leſte hapely thynke diſpleaſe ī ende fyrſte pleaſed euery affeccyon deſyre mannes herte ſemeth good holy nat forhwith folowed euery contrarious affeccion deſyre nat haſtely refuſed ſomtyme ryght expedyent man refrayne affeccions deſyres though good leſte happely importunite fall vnquyetnes mynde letted ſo fayle ī ſomtyme behoueth v vſe vyolence ſelfe ſtrongly reſyſt breke downe ſenſual appetyt nat regarde fleſhe wyll wyll nat alway take hede made ſubiecte wyll ſpirite ſo longe chaſtyſed cōpelled ſerue tyll redy al thing ſoule cōmaūdeth lerne contente lytell delyght ſymple thynges nat murmur ne grudge cōtrarious thinger may befall vnto ❧howe ſhulde kepe pacyence contynually ſtryue agaynſte al concupiſcence xiii chapyter lorde god ſay pacyence muche neceſſary vnto many contraryous thinges fall dayly lyfe ſe well howe ſo euer order ſelf haue pea yet lyfe nat without ſome batayle ſorowe ☞ ſone true thou ſayeſt wherfor wyll nat thou ſeke haue ſuche peace wanteth temptacions feleth nat ſome contradiccyon thou trowe beleue thou haſte founde peace whan thou haſte many trouble arte proued many cōtrarious thynges worlde yf thou ſaye thou mayſte nat ſuffre ſuche thynges howe ſhalt thou ſuffre fyre purgatory two euyl • e leſſe euyll taken suffre therfore pacyently lytell paynes thys worlde thou mayſt eſcape greater worlde come troweſt thou worldly men ſuffre litel nothynge yes truely thou ſhalte fynde none without ſome trouble thoughe thou ſeke moſte delycate perſones percaſe thou ſayeſt vnto agayne haue many delectacyons folow theyr owne pleaſures ſo muche pōder lytell theyr aduerſite wyl well thou ſayeſt haue al deſyre howe longe troweſt thou ſhall endure sothely ſhall ſodaynly vanyſſhe awaye ſmoke ayre ſo ſhall nat left remembraunce theyr ioyes paſſed yet whan lyued nat without great bytternes grefe oftē time ſame thing wherin theyr greateſt pleaſure receyued greate trouble payne ryghtewyſely came vnto aſmoche worldely people perceyue nat ne wyl nat perceyue dombre beaſtes· lyt • pleaſure thys corruptyble lyfe rēne hedlyng euerlaſtynge deth ♣ therfore ſone go nat thou thy concupycenſe tourne lyghtly thyne owne wyll delyte god fixe thy loue ſtrongely hym ſhall gyue aſkyng thy herte thou wylt haue conſolacyon abundantly wylte receyue ſothfaſt comfort cōmeth god dyſpoſe thy ſelfe fully diſpiſe thys worlde put hooly inordynate delectacyon thou ſhalte haue plentuouſly comforte god thou withdraweſt conſolacyon creature ſwete bleſſed conſolaciōs ſhalte thou receyue thy creatoure ſothly thou canſte nat fyrſte come ſuche conſolacyons heuynes laboure going thy olde cuſtome wyll ſomwhat ſtande better cuſtome yf may ouercome fleſſhe wyll murmure agaynſte feruoure ſpirite ſhalbe refrayned olde aūcyent enemye fende wyll let yf cā deuout prayer ſhalbe dryuen alwaye good bodely ghoſtely labour hys way ſhalbe ſtopped ſo ſhall nat dare nyghe vnto ❧of obedyence meke ſubiect example lorde ieſu chriſte xiiii chapyter mi ſone ſayth ſauyour chriſt laboureth withdrawe hym obedyence withdrawethe hym fro grace ſeketh haue pryuate thynges leſeth thynges cōmon man nat gladly ſubmytte hym hys ſuperyoure token fleſhe nat yet fully obedyent ſpirite ofte rebelleth murmureth therfore thou deſyre ouercome thy ſelfe make thy fleſſhe obeye mekely wyl ſpirite lerne firſt obey gladly thy ſuperiour warde enemy ſoner ouercome inner man ſoule nat febled waſtede worſe ne none greuous enemye ſoule thy ſelfe yf thy fleſhe nat well agreyng wyll ſpirite behoueth therfore haue true diſpiſing contempte thy ſelfe yf thou wylt preuayle agaynſte thy fleſhe blode aſmoche thou yet loueſt thy ſelfe inordynatly therfore thou feareſt reſigne thy wyll holy mannes wyll greate thynge arte duſte nought yf thou ſubdue thy ſelfe man ſake whā myghty mooſte highe god maker thynges ſubdued ſelfe mekelye manne thy ſake made ſelfe mooſte meke moſte lowe men thou ſhuldeſt lerne ouercome thy pryde throughe mekenes lerne therfore thou aſhes tractable learne thou earthe duſte meke bowe thy ſelfe vnder euery mannes ſo • e ſake learne breake thyne owne wyll ſubiecte mene thy herte ryſe greate wrath agaynſt thy ſelfe ſuffre nat pryde reygne ſhewe thy ſelfe ſo lytell ſo obedyent ſo noughty thyne owne ſyght thynkes men may ryghtwyſely go ouer trede vpon vpon erthe clay vayne man haſte thou complayne thou ſoule ſynner mayſte thou ryghtwyſely ſay agaynſte thē reproue ſyth thou haſte ſo ofte offended god haſte alſo ſo ofte deſerued paynes hell neuertheles eye mercye hath ſpared thy ſoule precyous ſyght thou ſhuldeſſe therby knowe greate loue haue therfore thankfull agayne gyue thy ſelfe parfyte true ſubieccion mekenes • e redy herte paciētly ſuffre ſake thyne owne cōtemptes diſpiſingꝭ whā ſo euer ſhall happen fall vnto amen ❧of ſecrete hyd iugementes god conſydered nat proued good dedes xv chapiter lorde thou ſowneſte thy iugementes terryblye vppon fylleſte bodye bone greate feare drede ſoule alſo trembleth ſore greatly aſtonyed ſe heuenes bene nat cleane thy ſyght ſythe thou foundeſte defaut angelles ſparedeſt nat ſhall become yt vyle ſtynkyng careyne sterres fell heuen duſte aſſhes ſhulde preſume alſo ſome people ſemed haue great werkes vertue haue fallen full lowe ſuche fedde meate angel haue ſene delyte ſwynes meate ſay fleſſhly pleaſures wherfore maye wel ſayde verified holynes ne goodnes v yf thou withdrawe thy hande mercye v ne wyſdome maye auayle v ★ thou lorde gouerne nat ne ſtrēgth helpe yf thou ceiſe preſerue v ne ſure chaſtyte yf thou lorde defende nat ne ſure kepynge many profyte v yf thou lorde nat wakery vpon v yf forſaken anone drowned peryſſhe yf thou lytell vyſyte v thy grace anone lyue lyfte vp agayne vnſtable confermed colde dull ſtyrred feruoure ſpiryte howe mekely howe abiectely ought therfore fele ſelfe howe muche ought herte dyſpyſe ſelfe thoughe holdē neuer ſo good holy ſyght worlde howe profoundely ought ſubmytte thy depe hym ſelfe pryde whome trouth god hath perfytely made ſubiecte vnto hym ne maye nat deceyued flateryng putteth hole truſte god ſeeth wel ſpeake vayne nought ſhall ſhortely fayle ſounde wordes trouth god alwaye abydeth ❧howe man ſhall ordre hym ſelfe hys deſyres xvi chapiter mi ſonne ſaythe sauyour chriſte thus ſhalte thou ſaye euery thynge thou deſyreſte lorde yf thy wyll done aſke yf thy prayſinge fulfylled thy name yf thou ſe good profytable gyue grace vſe thy honoure ♣ yf thou knowe hurtefull nat profytable helth ſoule take ſuche deſyre euery deſyre cōmeth nat holy ghoſte thoughe ſeme ryght wyſe good ſomtyme full herde iudge whether good ſpiryte euell ſpirite moueth thynge whether thou moued thyne owne ſpiryte many deceyued ende whiche fyrſte ſemed haue bene moued holy ghooſte therfore dreade god mekenes herte deſyre aſke ſo euer cōmeth mynde deſyred aſked hole forſakynge ſelfe cōmyte thynges god ſay thus ★ lorde thou knoweſt thynge mooſte profytable thy wyll gyue thou wylte muche thou wylte whan thou wylte thou knoweſte beſt done ſhall pleaſe ſhalbe moſte thy honour put thou wylte frely thynges thy wyll thy creature thy handes lede tourne thou wylte lo thy ſeruaunte redy al thynges thou cōmaundeſt deſyre nat lyue ſelfe wolde god myght worthely profytably thy honoure amen ❧a prayer wyll god alwaye fulfylled xvii chapytre mooſte benygne lorde ieſu graūt power wyll nat wyll thou wylte wyll nat graūte may dye thyngꝭ worlde loue diſpiſed man vnknowen thys worlde graunte alſo aboue thynges deſyred may reſte fully pacyfye herte thou lorde arte true peace herte parfyte reſte body ſoule without thynges greuous vnquyet wh •• fore peace tha • one hygh one bleſſed one endles goodnes ſhall alwaye reſte ſo mo • amen ❧that true ſolace conforte god xviii chapytre ſo euer may deſyre thinke cōforte abyde nat truſte haue herafter alone myght haue ſolace cōforte worlde myght vſe delytes thereof myne owne deſyre without ſynne certayne myght nat longe endure wherfore ſoule may fully cōforted ne perfytely refreſſhed god cōforter poore ſpiryt embracer meke lowe herte abyde ſoule abyde promyſe god thou ſhalte haue abundaūce al goodnes heuen thou inordinatly coueyte theſe goodꝭ p̄ſent thou ſhalte leſe goodnes eternal haue therfore goodꝭ preſent • ſe eternal deſire thou mayſte maner ſacyate temporall goodes far thou arte nat create vſe reſtethe yf thou alone myghteſt haue goodes euer create made thou mighteſte nat therfore happy bleſſed thy bleſſed fulnes thy full felicite ſtandeth onely god hath made thynges nought nat ſuche felicite cōmended folyſſhe louers worlde ſuche good cryſten men woman hope haue bleſhe heuen ſome ghoſtely perſons clene pure herte ſomtyme taſte thys preſent lyfe whoſe conuerſacyon heuen worldly ſolace euery place euery tyme ſpecyal ſolace gladely thy loue wante mannes ſolace yf thy ſolace want alſo thy wyll thy ryghtwyſe prouynge aſſayinge may ſynguler conforte hyghe ſolace thou ſhalte nat alwaye angry ne thou ſhalte nat alway threte ſo mo • amen ❧that ſtudy buſynes mynde ought put god xix chapitre mi ſonne hathe lorde ſeruaunt • ſuffre wyll knowe beſt moſte expediēt thou workeſt ī many glad hym wyll delyuer frō anguyſhe ſorowe come lorde come without haue glade daye ne houre thou arte al ioye gladnes without ſoule barayne voyde wretche maner pryſon bounde fetter tyll thou throughe thou lorde god hope euerlaſtynge helthe ſhall nat ceſſe prayer tyll thy grace retourne agayne thou ſpeake inwardely ſoule ſaye thus lo come thou haſte called thy teares deſyres thy herte thy mekenes thy contricyō haue bowed downe brought ſhall ſaye agayne lorde haue called haue deſyred haue redy forſake thynges thou firſte haſte ſtyred ſeke wherfore thou alway bleſſed haſt ſhewed ſuch goodnes multytude mercy hath thy ſeruaunt lorde ſay meken hym ſelfe thy maieſte euer haue mynde hys owne iniquyte none lyke lorde heuen ne erthe thy warkes good thy iugementes ryghtwyſe thy prouydence thynges gouerned wherfore art wyſdome father euerlaſtynge ioye glory humbly beſeche bodye ſoule herte • onge thy creature may alwaye laude bleſſe amen ❧of remembrynge greate manyfolde benefaytes god xxiiii hys loue perfytely fully oned god ſo euer ſo euer hauee vertue conning litell worth afore god therfore ſhall haue lytell vertue longr ſhall lye ſtyll earthely thynges accomptethe thinge great worthy prayeſd onely god thynges beſydes god nought nought accompted great differēce betwene wyſ • ome deuoute man lyghtned grace connynge ſubtyll ſtudyous clerke lernynge muche noble muche worthy cometh influence gracyous gyft god thā goten labour ſtudy mā many deſyre haue gyfte contemplacyon wyll nat vſe ſuche thinges requyred cōtemplacion one great let contemplacion ſtande ſo longe outwarde ſygnes inſenſyble thinges take hede perfyte mortifyeng body ſpirite wote nat howe ne ſpirite led ne pretende called ſpirituall perſones take greter laboure ſtudy tranſytory thynges knowe inwarde ſtate owne ſoule ala ſorow anone haue made lytell recolleccyon god renne forth outwarde thynges nat ſerche owne conſcyence due examynacyon ſhulde ne hede nat affeccion reſteth ne folowe nat dedes ſo euyll ſo vncleane people corrupted thēſelfe fleſſhely vnclennes therfore folowed great flode verely whā inwarde affeccion corrupted neceſſary dedes folouinge therupon alſo corrupted cleane herte ſpringeth frute good lyfe ofte tymes aſked dedes ſuche man hath done zele entent dyd thē lytell regarded whether man ryche ſtronge fayre able good writer good ſynger good labourer ofte enquyred howe poore nat deceyued ❧howe ſhulde forſake ſelfe thurſte downe couetyſe herte xxxvii chapitre mi ſonne ſaythe oure lorde thou ſhalte nat haue perfyte lybertye mynde hooly forſake thy ſelfe propryetayres louers theym ſelfe coueytous perſones curyous vayne gloryous renners alſo ſuche ſeke thinges ſofte delectable worlde nat ieſu chriſte ofte faynynge gredely ſykynge thingꝭ ſhall nat longe endure men fetered bounden cheynes haue perfyte lyberty ne fredome ſpirite thinges ſhall peryſſhe nat wroughte god holde well thy mynde ſhorte worde forſake thinges thou ſhalte fynde thinges ſake couetyſe thou ſhalte fynde great reſte prynte well ī thy minde haue ſayde whā thou haſte fulfylled thou ſhalte well knowe true ♣ lorde thys leſſon nat one dayes worke ne play chyldren conteyned full perfeccion religion alſo ſone thou oughteſte nat tourned fro god ne thinge dyſcouraged frō hys ſeruyce whā thou hereſte ſtrayte lyfe perfyte men rather thou oughteſt prouoked therby hygher perfeccion leſte deſyre ī herte thou myghteſt come therto wolde god thou fyrſte come poynt thou nat louer thy ſelf thou woldeſte kepe commaundementes cōmaundemētes hym haue appoynted thy father ſpirituall thou ſhuldeſte pleaſe greatly thy lyfe ſhuldeſte paſſe forth ioye peace thou haſte yet many thynges forſake whiche thou hooly forſake thou ſhalt nat get thou deſyreſte therfore counſayle bye bryght ſhyninge golde ſaye heuenly wyſdome diſpyſeth earthly thynges caſte fro worldy wyſdome mannes conforte thyne owne affeccyons thou choſe haue vile thinges abiecte rather precious hygh ſyght worde true heuenly wyſdome ſemeth many vyle lytell well nyghe forgotten many ſaye theyr mouthe good nat deſyre magnified ye worlde theyr lyfe foloweth nat theyr ſaying therfore deſire priuely herte yet precyous margarete hyghe vertue hyd fro moche people theyr preſumpcion get ſo may ❧of vnſtablenes mannes herte fynall intent thynges ſhulde god xxviiii chapitre mi ſonne loke thou byleue nat thyne owne affeccyon changeth ofte one lōge thou lyueſt thou ſhalt ſubiecte chaūge habilyte whether thou wylt nat nowe glad nowe ſorowfull nowe pleaſed nowe dyſpleaſed nowe deuoute nowe vndeuout nowe luſty nowe ſlouthful nowe heuy nowe lightſōe wife man wel taughte ghoſtely trauayle ſtandeth ſtable ſuche thinges forſeth lytell feleth ne ſyde wynde vnſtablenes bloweth intēte ſtudy hys mynde howe maye moſte profyte vertue hooly dyrected god whiche graunte v amen ❧howe lorde god ſauoureth hys louer ſwetely aboue thynges al thynges xxxix chapitre ovre lorde ſayth ſo wolde haue deſyre ☞o thys ſauoury worlde ſwete ſaye lorde hym loueth worde nat worlde hym vnderſtādeth worde ſayde inough yet repete ofte lykynge loueth maye therfore playnly ſpeke mater ſay lorde whā thou arte preſent thinge pleſaunte lykynge whan thou arte abſente thinge greuous greately myſlykynge whan thou cōmeſ • e thou makeſte myne herte reſtfull bryngeſt newe ioye thou makeſte thy louer fele vnderſtande trouthe haue true iugemente thynges al thinges laude prayſe ★ lorde without nothing may longe lykynge ne pleaſaunt thynge ſhulde lykynge ſauoury muſte helpe thy grace tempered ſpicerie thy wyſdome hym whome thou ſauoureſt well ſhall nat ſauoure well hym thou ſauoureſte nat well vnto maye ioyfull lykynge worldly wyſe men ſauoure fleſſhely delytes fayle thys wyſdome worldly wyſdome founde greate vanyte fleſſhely pleaſures euer laſtynge deathe therfore folowe lorde diſpiſyng ſhorde perfyte mortifyēge theyr fleſhely luſtes knowen wyſe led fro vanyte trouth fro fleſſhly lykynge ſpiryuall clennes ſuche perſones god ſauoureth wonder ſwete ſo euer fynde creature referre laude prayſynge theyr creatoure ſe well great difference betwyxt creature creatoure eternyte tyme betwyxte lyghte made lyght vnmade euerlaſtynge lyghte farre paſſynge thynges made ★ sende downe beames thy lyghtenyngs frome aboue purifye gladde clarifie inwarde party herte quycken ſpirite al power therof maye cleue faſte ioyned ioyfull gladnes ghoſtely rauyſſhynges ☞ whan ſhall bleſſed houre come thou ſhalte vyſyte gladde thy bleſſed preſence ſo thou longe gyfte nat gyuen thou ſhall ful ioy ala ſorowe mine olde man fleſhely lykinge yet lyueth nat yet fully crucifyed parfitely deed yet ſtriueth fleſhe ſtrongely againſt ſpirite moueth great inwarde batayle agaynſte ſuffereth nat kyngdome ſoule lyue peace thou good lorde haſte lordeſhype ouer power ſee doſte aſſwage ſtremes flouinges aryſe helpe breke downe power myn enemy alwaye moue batayle shewe greatnes thy goodnes let power thy ryght hande glorified none hope refuge onely lorde god whome ioye honoure glorye euerlaſtyngly amen ❧that full ſuretye fro temptacyon lyfe xl chapitre ovr lorde ſayth hys ſeruaunte thus thou ſhalte neuer ſeker fro temtacyon tribulacyon lyfe therfore armoure ſpirytuall ſhall alway longe thou lyueſt neceſſary thou arte amonge thyne enemyes ſhalt troubled vexed euery ſyde thou vſe euery place ſhelde pacyence thou ſhalt nat longe kepe vnwoūded ouer yf thou ſet nat thy herte ſtrongly redy wyll ſuffre thinges pacyently thou mayſt nat longe bere ardoure ne come vnto rewarde bleſſed ſayntes behoueth therfore māly paſſe ouer many thynges vſe ſtronge hande agaynſte obieccyons enemye ouercomer promyſed angelles fode hym ouercome lefte moche myſery thou ſeke reſte thys lyfe howe ſhalte thou come reſt euerlaſting set nat thy ſelfe haue reſte haue pacyence ſeke true ſouthfaſte reſte nat erth heuen nat man ne creature god onely wher loue god thou oughteſt ſuffre gladly al thinges ſay laboures ſorowes tēptacions vexacyons anguyſhes nedenes ſykenes iniuries euyll ſaynges repreuynges oppreſſyons confuſions correccions diſpyſynges theſe helpe man greatly vertues theſe proue true knyght chryſte make redy hym heuenly crowne lorde ſhal yelde hym agayne euerlaſtynge rewarde ſhorte laboure infynyte glory tranſytory confuſyon troweſte thou thou ſhalt haue alway ſpirituall confortes thy wyll nay nay ſaintꝭ thē nat many great grefs dyuers temptacyons great deſolacions pacyence truſted thē ſelfe knewe wel paſſions thys worlde nat able ſelfe get glory ordeyned thē ī kyngdome heuen wylte thou loke haue anone myghte vnnethes gette afore greate wepynges laboures abyde pacyently cōmynge lorde manfully hys bidding conforted hym myſtruſte hym nat ne go nat backe fro ſeruyce payne ne drede lay forthe thy body ſoule pacyence mekenes agaynſte al thyngꝭ myght vntruly ſpoken agaynſte hym neuertheles ſōtyme anſwered agayne leſte hys ſcyence hurte hynderaūce myght haue growē arte thou dredeſt ſo ſore mortall man day morowe appereth nat drede god thou ſhalt nat nede drede man maye man wordes iniuries hurteth hym ſelfe ende ſhall ne fle iugement god ſo euer haue alwaye good eye thy ſoule ſtryue nat agayne knowen fewe yet true erreth nat ne yet maye nat erre thoughe ſyght ſome vnwyſe perſones ſemeth nat ſo ★ therfore euery doute behoueth rene nat leaue muche vnto thyne owne reaſon euery thing ſhall ſende contente ryghtwyſe man neuer troubled thynge ſhall ſuffre fall vnto hym ſo much though thing vntruely ſpoken agaynſte hym ſhulde nat muche care ne ſhulde nat muche ioy thoughe ſomtyme reaſonably excuſed thynketh alway ſercheth mannes herte iuge nat outwarde apparaunce ofte tymes ſhal founde ſyght worthy blamed mānes ſyght ſemeth muche worthy prayſed lorde god moſte ryghtwyſe iuge ſtronge pacyente whiche knoweſte fraylte malyce man thou ſtrength hole conforte neceſſyties myne owne conſcyence lorde ſuffyſeth nat thou knoweſte knowe nat therfor ī euery reprofe ought alway meken ſelfe verely thou arte preſent ſacramente god man ★ thou wylte therfore ſhall receyue knitte ſelfe vnto inperfyte charyte wherfore aſke mercy deſyre thou gyue thy ſpecyall grace maye fro henſe forth fully molten relented flowe thy loue neuer intermytte ſelfe cō forte thys moſt hygh moſt worthy ſacrament lyfe ſoule body▪ medecyne al ſpiritual ſykenes whereby vyces cured paſſyons refrayned temptacyōs ouercome demynyſſhed greatier grace ſen • e vertue encreaſed fayth ſtablyſſhed hope ſtrengthed charyte kyndeled ſpred abrode thou haſt gyuen yet ofte tymes gyueſte many greate gyftes ſacramente thy beloued ſeruauntes deuoutly receyue thou thereby arte ſtronge vpholder ſoule repayrer infyrmyties man gyuer inwarde conſolacion cōforte tribulacion fro depenes theyr owne de • ection thou lay • eſt thē agayne ſtrōg hope thy preſeruacyon reneweſte lyghteſt inwardely newe grace ſo felte thē ſelfe receyuynge bleſſed ſacramēt heuy without affec • ion whan haue receyued haue founde ſelfe chaunged great ghoſtely feruoure al thou doſte vnto thy electe people thy greate goodnes may ſe knowe openly experience haue nothynge thē ſelfe grace goodnes haue haue receyued ſelfe colde dull vndeuout made feruente quycke ſpirite deuoute folowers thy wyll may go mekely fountayne ſwetenes ſhall brynge awaye hym greate plentye ſwetneſſe may ſtande greate fyre ſhall fele greate hete thereof thou lorde arte fountayne ſwetneſſe fyre alwayes brennynge neuer faylynge therfore thoughe maye nat drawe thy fulnes foūtayne ne drynke therof full ſhall neuer leſſe put mouthe hole heuenly pype may take ſome litel droppe thereof refreſſhe thurſte ſo nat dryed awaye thoughe nat heuenly brennyng charite seraphyns cherubyns neuertheles ſhall endeuer ſet ſelfe deuocyon prepayre myne herte maye get ſome lytell ſparkle brennynge heuenly lyue though meke receyuīg thys lyuely ſacrament ſo euer wanteth beſeche lorde ieſu moſte holy bleſſed thou benyngly gracyouſly ſupply thou haſte vouchedſafe call thy ſayenge come ye laboure charged ſhall refreſſhe ★ laboure ſwete body turmented ſorowe herte charged ſynnes trauayled temptacyons intriked oppreſſed many euyll paſſyons none may helpe maye delyurr ne may make ſaufe thou lorde god ſauyoure whome cōmytte myne thou kepe lede lyfe euerlaſtyng accepte take laude glorye thy name haſte ordayned thy body blode meate drynke graunte lorde beſeche ofte receyuynge thy highe myſtery feruoure deuocyon may dayly encreaſe ❧of worthynes ſacramente aulter ſtate preeſthode v chapiter thou haddeſt ye purete angel holines ſaynt iohn̄ baptiſt thou ſhuldeſt nat yt worthy receyue ne touche holy ſacramente nat graunted merytes man man ſhulde cōſecrate touche ſacrament chriſte take meate breade angel greate miſterye great dignyte preeſtes whome graunted nat graunted angelles preſtes onely • e duely ordayned churche haue power ſynge maſſe canſecrate bodye chryſte preeſte minyſter god vſynge worde conſecracion cōmaundement ordinaunce god god pryncypall doer inuiſyble worker whome ſubiecte wylleth obeyeth commaundeth thou oughteſt therfore beleue almyghty god moſte excellent ſacrament thā thyne owne wytte vyſible token ſygne therfore drede reuerence go bleſſed werke take hede diligently ſe fro whens myſtery ſeruyce commeth gyuen vnto touchyng handes byſſhope thou arte nowe made preeſte arte cōſecrate ſynge maſſe take hede therfore thou faythfully deuoutely offre thy ſacryfyce god due tyme thou kepe thy ſelfe without reprofe thou haſt nat made thy bourden light▪ thou arte nowe boūde ſtrayter bonde dyſcyplyne muche hyghe perfeccion thou preeſte ought adourned vertues gyue example good lyfe hys conuerſacyon ſhulde nat cōmon people ne comon way worlde angel heuen perfyte men erthe • e moſte beſte diſpoſed ſerue god preeſte alſo clothed hooly veſtementes bereth place chryſte ſhulde humbly mekely pray lorde hym ſelfe people hath hym behynde ſygne croſſe chryſte dylygently ſhulde remembre hys paſſyon beareth hym croſſe may dilygently beholde ſe ye ſteppes chryſte ſtudy feruently folowe behynde hym alſo ſygned croſſe ſhulde gladly mekely ſuffre aduerſityes loue god bereth croſſe hym ſhulde bewayle hys owne ſynnes bearethe behynde hym may cōpaſſyon bewepe ſynnes knowe hym ſelfe ſet meane betwene god people nat ceaſe prayer holy oblacyō tyl may deſerue almyghty god mercy grace whan preeſte ſaythe maſſe honoureth god maketh angel glad edifieth churche helpeth people lyue gyueth reſte theym deed maketh hym ſelfe parte taker good dedes ❧of inwarde remembraunce exercyſe man ought haue afore receyuing body chriſt vi chapitre lorde whan thynke thy worthynes great fylthynes tremble ſtrongly confounded ſelfe yf receyue nat fle eternall lyfe yf vnworthely receyue rēne thy wrath ſhall good lorde helper protectoure conforter ryght ſure counſayloure neceſſites ★ teache good lorde ryghte waye purpoſe vnto ſome redy exc • rcyſe couenable vnto receyuynge holy myſtery neceſſary vnto greatly profytable knowe howe deuoutly reuerently oughte prepayre myne herte receyue conſecrate ſo greate ſo goodely ſacrifiſe ❧of dyſcuſſynge owne conſcyence purpoſe amendemente viii chapiter behoueth aboue thynges ſoueraygne reuerence profounde mekenes hert full faythe humble intent • honoure god celebrate take receyue thys hooly ſacramente examyne dilygentely thy conſcyence true contrycyon meke confeſſyon make cleane thy power ſo thou knowe nothynge greueth byteth thy conſcyence maye let go frely vnto haue dyſpleaſure thy ſynnes generall thy dayly exceſſes offence haue ſyghynges ſorowyngꝭ ſpeciall tyme wyll ſuffre confeſſe vnto god ſecrete thyne herte miſeryes thy paſſyons wepe ſorowe thou arte yet ſo carnall worldely ſo mortyfied fro thy paſſyons ſo full mocyons concupiſcences ſo vnware ſo euyll ordered thy outwarde wyttes ſo ofte intryked vayne fantaſies ſo muche enclyned outwarde worldly thynges ſo neglygent inwarde thynges ſo redy laughynge dyſſolucyon ſo harde wepynge cōpunccion ſo redy eaſy thynges lykyng fleſhe ſo ſlowe penaunce feruoure ſpirite ſo curious newe thynges ſe fayre thinges ſo loth meke abiecte thynges ſo couetous haue muche ſo ſcarſe gyue ſo glad holde ſo vnaduyſed ſpeking ſo incontynent ſtyll ſo euyll ordered maners ſo importune dedes ſo gredy vpō meate ſo defe worde god ſo quycke reſte ſo ſlowe laboure ſo attētyue fable ſo ſlepy holy vigels haſty ende ſo vnſtable take hede vnto waye ende ſo neclygente ſeruyce god ſo dulie ſo vndeuoute go maſſe ſo drye thy howſen ſo ſone fallen large outwarde thinges ſo ſeldome gathered gether inwarde thinges ſo ſone moued angre wrathe ſo lyghtely ſtyred dyſpleaſure ſo redy iuge ſo rygorous reproue ſo glad proſperyte ſo feble aduerſyte ſo • te purpoſynge many good thynges ſo ſyldome bryngynge effecte whā thou haſte thus confeſſed bewepte theſe defautes ſuche lyke great ſorowe diſpleaſure thine owne fraylnes ſet full purpoſe amende thy lyfe profyte alwaye fro better better full reſygngne hole wyll offre thy ſelfe honoure name aulter thy herte ſacrafyce ſay faythfull cōmyttīg bothe thy body ſoule ſo thou mayſt worthy offre hygh ſacryfice receyue helthfully ſacramente holy body oblacyon worthy ſatiſfaccyon greater put away ſynne man offre ſelfe purely hooly god offerynge body chryſte maſſe holy cōmunyon man truely penytente ofte cometh grace forgyuenes lorde ſayth nat deth ſynner rather cō uerted lyue ſhall remembre ſynnes inuyſyble may helth helth people lorde offre ſynnes offence haue commytted thy holy aungels fro day myghte fyrſte offende vnto thys daye thou voucheſaufe thy great charite put away al ſynnes clenſe conſcience myne offence reſtore agayne grace ſynne haue loſt thou forgyue thynges paſte receyue mercyfully bleſſed kyſſyng peace forgyuenes may mekely confeſſe bewayle ſinnes continually aſke mercy forgyue mercyfull lorde nowe beſeche al ſyn̄es diſpleaſe muche wyll neuer cō mytte agayne ſorowe redy penaūce ſatiſfaccyon power forgyue lorde forgyue ſynnes thy holy name ſaue ſoule yt thou haſte redemed thy precyous blode cōmytte ſelfe holy vnto thy mercy reſygne thy handes thy goodneſſe nat malyce wretchedneſſe offre alſo vnto good dedes though fewe imparfyte thou amende ſanctifye make lykynge acceptable alway make better better thou brynge though • ſlowe vnprofytable perſon bleſſed laudable ende ♣ offer alſo deſyres deuoute perſones neceſſyte myne aunceſters frendes brother ſyſter louers thy loue haue done good haue deſyred aſked praye ſacryfyce theyr frendes whether lyue dede may rather fele thy helpe thy grace gyft thy heuenly conſolacyon thy proteccyon fro peryls delyueraunce fro payne ſo beynge delyuered fro euyls maye ſpyrytuall gladneſſe yelde hyghe laude prayſynges offre alſo prayer peaſyble offerynge haue thynge hyndered made heuye haue done hurte greue theym alſo whome haue tyme made heuy troubled greued ſclaundered wordes dede wittyngly ignoraūtly thou forgyue v together ſynnes offence agaynſt eche v againſt thou lorde take fro hertes al ſuſpicion indignacyon wrathe varyaunce ſo euer may let charyte dimyniſſhe ye fraternal loue eche v ſhulde haue hauē mercy lorde haue mercy aſke mercy gyue grace thē haue nede make v ſtande ſuche caſe worthy haue thy grace fynally come lyfe euerlaſtynge amen ❧that holy communyon nat lyghtely forborne x chapiter behoueth renne ofte fountayne grace mercye fountayne goodnes puryte thou mayſt heled fro paſſyons vyces made ſtrongt againſt temptacyons deceytfull craftes enemye fyue knowynge greateſte frute hygheſte remedy receyuynge thys bleſſed ſacramēt enforſeth hym wayes let withdrawe faythfull ouer muche fearefull perplexed ſo may dymynyſſhe theyr affeccyon take away theyr faythe haply may therby make eyther vtterly ceaſe fro beynge howſeled el go lytel deuocyō nat thīg care hys craftes ouer great doute makyng confeſſyon letteth muche holy purpoſe therfore coūſayle wyſe men put away doutfulnes ſcripulouſnes let grace god dyſtroye holly deuocyon thy mynde alſo nat good lytell trouble grefe thou leue thys holy worke go lyghtly confeſſed forgyue gladly haue offended yf thou haue offēded mekely aſke forgyueneſſe god ſhall right mercyfully forgyue profyteth longe tary fro cōfeſſyon dyffer holy communyon pourge fyrſt quyckely caſt thy venyme haſt take thy medecyne thou ſhall fele profyte therby thā thou taryeddeſt lenger fro yf thou differre day fro thinge morowe may happen come greatter ſo thou mayſt let longe fro thy good purpoſe made afterwarde vnapte vnto therfore ſone thou canſte diſcharge thy ſelfe fro ſuche heuynes dulnes mynde fro ſlouch nothynge profyteth longe anguyſſhed longe go trouble ſequeſter hym ſelfe ſuche dayly obſtacles fro yt deuyne myſteryes doth great hurte commonly bryngeth great ſlouth lacke deuocyon ala ſorowe ſome ſlouthfull diſſolute perſones gladely ſeke cauſes tary fro confeſſyon ſo dyfferre longer holy cōmunyon entente ſhulde nat boūde gyue ſelfe ſure kepyng thē ſelfe time come thā haue done ala howe lytell charyte ſlender ſpirituall cōmunion chriſte ſaye remēbrynge paſſyon neuertheles certayne dayes tymes bounde receyue ſacramentally body hys redemoure great reuerence rather pretende therein laude honoure god owne lyueſte thou oughteſt nat ſhulde greue make thē tedyous kepe comon waye ordynaūce holy father rather confyrme thy ſelfe ſhalbe profytable folow thyne owne deuocion pryuate pleſure ❧that body chryſt good cōſcyence thoughe may nat lyue ſo great innocencye ought yet gyue v grace leſt tha may wepe ſorowe euyls haue done ſo ſpiritual mekenes ful purpoſe good wyl may ſerue amen ❧that ſhalbe houſeled ought repayre hym ſelfe therto great dilygence xii chapiter louer purety lyberall gyuer holynes ſeke clene herte reſtyng place make redy great chambre ſtrawed thyne herte diſcyples ſhall kepe myne vpon thy offence greate bytterneſſe herte true louer wyll prepare hys beloued frende ye beſt fayreſt place knowen loue affeccyon hym receyueth frende neuertheleſſe knowe thou mayſte nat thy ſelfe ſuffyce make preparinge fully ought euery poynte thoughe thou wente hoole yere together haddeſt none thyng thy mynde thinke vpon mercye grace thou arte ſuffred go vnto table poore mā called dyner ryche man none thinge gyue hym agayne onely humble hym ſelfe thāke thy beſte dilygence nat onely cuſtome neceſſyte onely thou arte bounde drede reuerence greate affeccyon take body thy beloued lorde god ſo louyngly vouched ſaufe come vnto ☞❧ hathe called haue commaunded thynge ſhulde done ſhall ſupply wanteth come therfore receyue whan gyue ye grace deuociō yelde thankinges therfore nat yt thou art worthy haue yt haue ſhewed mercy louyngly yf thou haue nat grace deuocyon throughe receyuinge ſacramēt thou feleſte thy ſelfe drye vndeuoute thou yet contynewe ſtyll thy prayer wayle wept call grace ceaſe nat tyll thou mayſt receyue ſome lytell drope helthful grace deuocion thou haſt nede nat ne thou comeſte nat ſanctifie come ſanctifye make better thou thou commeſt ſanctified oned thou mayſte receyue newe grace kyndled newe amendemēt nat forget grace alwaye thy dylygence prepayre thy herte brynge thy beloued behoueth nat p̄payre thy ſelfe vnto deuociō thou ſhalt houſled thou alſo kepe thy ſelfe therein diligently receyuynge ſacrament leſſe kepynge requyſite deuoute preparacion nedefull good kepynge beſt p̄paracion receyue newe grace man ſhalbe vndiſpoſed thereto yf anone hath receyued ſacrament gyue hym ſelfe outwarde ſolace beware much ſpekynge abyde ſome ſecrete place kepe thy lorde god thou haſt hym worlde maye nat take whome thou muſte gyue ſo fro hen forth thou lyue nat thy ſelfe onely ❧that deuout ſoule ſhulde greatly deſyre hys herte onyed chriſt bleſſed ſacramente xiii chapiter ſhall graunt vnto lorde ye may fynde onely open al mine herte haue myne herte deſyreth ſo man may diſceyue creature moue drawe backe thou ſpeke louer wonte ſpeke beloued frende beloued frende pray deſyre maye hooly onyed maye withdrawe myne hert fro thynges create throughe holy cōmunion ofte ſayenge maſſe ſauer taſte eternall thynges ★ ah lorde god whan ſhall al onyed hooly molten thy loue ſo hooly forget ſelfe thou graūte may ſo abyde alway gether one verely thou arte beloued electe choſen ī whome ſoule coueyteth abyde dayes hys lyfe thou arte lorde peace whome ſufferayne peace true reſte whome laboure ſorowe infinite miſery verely thou art hyd god thy counſayle nat wycked people meke men ſymple herte howe ſwete howe benygne thy holy ſpiryte whiche intēt thou woldeſt ſhewe thy choſen people thy ſwetnes haſte vouchedſafe refreſſhe moſte ſwete breade dyſcendeth heuen verely none nacyon ſo great hath goddes ſo nyghe vnto thē thou lorde god arte thy faythfull people whome theyr dayly ſolace reyſe hertes loue heuenly thinges thou gyueſt thy ſelfe meate drynke ★ people ſo noble chryſten people creature vnder heuen ſo muche beloued deuoute chryſtē ſoule whome god entreth fedeth hys owne glorious fleſhe blode ☞ ineſtimable grace meruaylous worthines loue without meaſure ſyngulerly ſhewed vnto man ſhal yelde agayne god grace hyghe charyte truely nothing acceptable vnto hym hooly gyue hym myne herte inwardely ioyne ſelfe vnto ſhal myne inwarde partes ioy whā ſoule perfytely oned hym ſhal ſay thou wylt wyl ſhall anſwere hym agayne ſaye vouche ſaufe lorde abyde wyll gladly abyde al deſyre herte may faſte knyt vnto without departynge amen ❧of brennynge deſyre ſome deuoute perſones haue body chryſte xiiii cha howe great multitude ſwetneſſe lorde thou haſte hydde drede theym loue verely whan remembre many deuoute perſones haue come hooly ſacramente ſo great feruoure deuocyon many tymes aſtonyed confoūded ī ſelfe go vnto thy aulter table holy cōmunion ſo coldely ſo lytel feruour abyde ſtil ſo drye without affeccyon hert nat ſo hooly kyndeled lorde god ſo ſtrōgly drawen therby affeccion many deuoute perſones haue bene whiche greate deſyre haue hadde hooly communion feable loue herte haue thereto myght nat refrayne ſelfe wepynge effectuouſly mouthe theyr herte body gether opened mouthes lorde arte lyuely fountayne bicauſe coulde nat otherwyſe aſwage ne temper theyr hunger toke holy body whiche dyd great ioy ſpiritual gredines truely great brēuing faith probable argumēt thy holy preſence alſo knowe verely theyr lorde brekynge breade whoſe hertes ſo ſtrongly brenneth thē preſence lorde ieſu ſacramentally walkynge verely ſuche affeccion deuocion ſo ſtronge feruour loue ofte tyme farre thou therfor moſte ſwete benygne lorde ieſu mercifull meke vnto graunt thy poore ſeruaunt may fele ſomtyme ſome lytel part harty affeccyon thy loue thys holy cōmunyon fayth maye recouer amende myne hope thy goodnes perfite charite beynge one perfitly kyndeled hauynge experyence heuenly manna neuer fayle thy mercy lorde ſtronge ynoughe graunt thys grace ſo muche deſyre whan tyme thy pleaſure ſhal come beningly viſite ſpirite brennyng feruour thoughe nat brenne ſo greate deſyre ſuche ſpecyall deuoute perſones haue done yet neuertheleſſe haue deſyre thy grace inflamed brēnyng deſyre prayeng deſyryng may made parte taker ſuche thy feruēt louers nombred theyr holy cōpany ❧that grace deuocyon gotten throughe mekenes forſakynge ſelfe xv chapiter behoueth abydyngly ſeke grace deuocyon without ceaſynge aſke pacyently fathfully abyde fully receyue mekely kepe ſtudiouſly work hooly cōmytte god tyme maner heuenly viſytacyon tyll pleſure ſhalbe come vnto pryncypally thou oughteſte meke whan thou felyſte lytell inwarde deuocyon thou ſhalte nat ouermuch caſte downe therfore inordynately heuy lorde giueth many tymes ſhorte momente denyed longe tyme gyueth alſo ſomtyme ende begynnynge prayour deferred graunte yf grace ſhulde alwayes anone graūted ſhulde anone preſente wyll hym aſketh ſhulde nat well able borne weke feble perſon therfore good hope meke pacyence grace deuocyon abydden taryed thou oughteſte arrecte thy ſelffe thyne owne ſynes whan grace nat giuē ſecretly taken fro somtyme lytell thinge letteth grace hydeth away may called lytell nat rather great letteth prohibiteth ſo good thynge whether lytell great thou amoue perfitely ouercome ſhall graunted vnto thou deſyreſt forthwith thou betakeſt thy ſelfe thyne herte god deſyreſt neyther thinge thyne owne pleaſure hooly putteſt thy wyll hys wyll thou ſhalte fynde thy ſelfe oned hym ſet ī great inwarde peace nothing ſhall ſauoure ſo well ſo muche pleaſe wyll pleaſure god fully done ſo euer therfore ī pure ſymple herte lyfte intent vp god voyde hym ſelfe fro inordinate loue diſpleaſure worldely thynge ſhall apte recyue grace ſhall beſte worthy haue gyfte deuocyon lorde giueth bleſſing fyndeth veſſels emptye voyde perfytely man renounce hym ſelfe worldly thynges diſpyſynge hym ſelfe drye ſelfe ſo much ſoner grace ſhall come ſhall plentuouſly entre hym hygher ſhall lyfte vp herte god herte ſhall ſe abounde ſhall meruayle delated hym ſelfe hande lorde hath holy put hande euer lo ſo ſhall man bleſſed ſeketh god herte taketh nat hys ſoule vayne suche man receyuing holy ſacrament deſerueth greate grace onyng god loketh nat owne deuocyon conſolacyon glory honoure god ❧that ſhulde open neceſſytes chryſte aſke hys grace xxi chapyter moſt ſwete lorde whome deſyre deuoutly receyue thou knoweſt ye infirmite neceſſite many ſynnes vyces lye howe ofte greued tempted troubled defouled come remedy make praiour cōforte ſpeke vnto hym knoweth thyngꝭ whome ſecrete inwarde thoughtes manyfeſte open whiche mayſte perfytly counſayle helpe thou knoweſt nede haue howe poore vertue lo ſtande poore naked aſkynge deſyryng thy grace refreſſhe therfor thy pooreſt ſeruaūt begging ſpiritual fode kyndle herte fyre thy loue illumyne blyndenes clerenes thy p̄ſence tourne worldly thinges bitternes al greuous thinges contraryous thynges pacience al create thinges diſpiſyng forgettyng lyfte vp myne herte heuen ſuffre nat lyue vaynly ne erre thys worlde thou lorde fro henſforthe ſhalte ſwete euer thou arte mete drinke loue ioye ſwetnes goodnes wolde god thou woldeſt kyndell inflame tourne hooly maye made one ſpirite grace īwarde oning meltyng brennynge loue ſuffre nat departe fro faſtyng drye worke mercyfully thou haſte ofte tymes meruaylouſly wrought thy beloued ſeruantes tyme paſte meruayle yf inflamed fayled ſelfe ſyth thou arte fyre alway brennynge neuer faylyng loue puryfyenge hertes lyghtenynge vnderſtandynge thy creature ❧of brennynge loue great affeccyon ſhulde haue receyue chryſte xvii chapiter hygh deuocyon brennynge loue feruoure affeccyon herte deſyre receyue lorde many ſayntꝭ deuoute perſones haue deſyred theyr cōmunyon moſte ſpecially pleaſed holynes theyr lyfe moſte brenning deuocion lorde god louer eternall goodnes felycyte without endyng coueyte receyue ye great deſyre due reuerēce holy man euer dyd myght though vnworthy haue ſuche felingꝭ deuo • yon yet neuetheles offre hole affeccyon herte verely yf onely brēning flamyng deſyres ouer meke mynde may ymagyne deſyre gyue offre hyghe reuerence worſhipe inwarde feruour deſyre reſerue thing ſelfe myne offre ī ſacrifyce frely moſt liberally alſo lorde god createur redemer wt ſuche affeccyon reuerē • laude honoure ſuche thankes dignite loue ſuche faythe hope puryte deſyre receyue thys daye thy moſt holy glorious mother virgyne mary deſyred receiued whā ſhe mekely deuoutly anſwered angel ſhewed myſtery thy incarnaciō ſaide ecce ancilla dn̄i fiat michi ſecundū verbū tuū ſay lo hande mayde god thy worde thy bleſſed precurſour ſaynte iohn̄ baptyſte moſte excellent ſayntꝭ glad ioyed great ioy ye holy ghoſt throughe thy
