ioye brenninge deuocion al reuerently deuoutly miniſter moſte hygh ſacramēt ful fayth receyue maye thereby deſerue fynde thy grace mercye whan haue obteyned deuocyon deſyred ſpirytually onyed therby wel cōforted meruaylouſly refreſſhed departed fro thy heuēly table wyl haue pore ſynner theyr remembraunce amen ❧that man ſhall nat curyous ſercher thys hooly ſacramente meke folower chriſte ſubduynge alway reaſon fayth xviii chapiter thou muſt beware curioꝰ vnprofitable ſerching thys moſt profounde ſacram̄t thou wylt nat drowned greate deppeth doutfulnes ſerchoure goddes mageſty ſhalbe anone thurſte glorye god power worke muche mā may vnderſtande neuertheles meke humble ſerchyng trouthe redy alway taught talke teachynge holy father ſufferable bleſſed ſymplicite leueth waye harde queſtyons goth playne ſtedfaſt way cōmaundementes god many haue loſte theyr deuocyon bycauſe wolde ſerche higher thingꝭ thā ꝑteyneth thē fayth good lyfe aſked na • hyghnes vnderſtāding depenes myſteryes god thou may nat vnderſtāde take ſuch thingꝭ within ye howe mayſt thou comp̄hende thoſe thingꝭ yt aboue ſubmitte thy ſelfe therfore mekely god ſubmytte alſo thy reaſon faith lyght knowlege true vnderſtā dynge ſhalbe gyuen vnto ſhalbe moſt profitable neceſſary ye ſome greuouſly tēpted fayth ſacrament nat reputed thē rather enemy therfore care nat diſput nat wt thy thoughtes anſwere nat ye doutꝭ yt thyne enemy ſhall laye vnto beleue wordis god beleue ſainctes prophetes ye wycken enemy ſhall fle away fro ofte tymes muche profitable ye ſeruauntes god ſhulde fele ſuſteyne ſuch doutes ꝓfe comonly ye enemye tempteth nat vnfaithful people ſīners whōe hath ſure poſſeſſyon tēpteth vexeth diuers maners faithful deuoute ꝑſons go therfore pure vndoubted fayth hūble reuerēce ꝓcede ſacramēt ſo euer thou canſt nat vnderſtāde cōmitte faythfully god god wyll nat deceyue ſhalbe deceyued truſteth ouermuche hymſelfe god walketh wt ſimple ꝑſons opened hīſelfe ſhewed himſelfe meke perſons gyueth vnderſtandyng thē poore ſpirite openeth ye wet pure clene myndes hydeth grace fro curyous mē proude mē mannes reſon feble weyke anone may deceyued faith ſtable true nat deceyued therfore reaſon al natural workyng muſte folowe faith without ferther reſoning faith loue moſt holy moſt excellēt ſacrament ſurmonte worke hygh ſecrete maner aboue reaſon eternal god lorde infinite power doth great thynges heuē earth yt may nat ſerched yf workes god ſuche might lyghtly vnderſtande mānes reaſon nat ſo meruaylous ſo ineſtimable ¶finis ❧a ſpirituall glaſſe rede diſtynctely ♣ pray rede engliſhe vnderſtande nat latyn tonge tranſlated laten englyſhe ſuch maner hereafter enſueth ſome bokes imprynted latter ende boke called laten imitacio chriſti ſaye englyſhe folowynge chryſte barnarde whiche ſente vnto yonge relygyous man whome muche loued called golden epiſtell wilderneſſe relygyon maye pleaſaunte ſwere vnto thou ſhalte nat ſyght hym founde vnkynde moſte mekely crucified ye counſaile yt nowe thou haſt takē vpon thou caſt nat lyghtely awaye leſte happely acceptable god thou take occupye thy place thou caſte ſtynkynge caryen conſyder therfore howe muche thou art bounde veraye true lambe chriſt whiche ledde offered ſacrifyce vppon aulter croſſe ſuffered many repreſſes mooſte harde ſcourgynges theym whome ſuche compaſſyon wept tenderly vppon ★ therfore thou mayſte attayne lyke thynge cal vnto thy lorde ieſu deuout prayer beſechynge hym thou mayſte true membre onyed throughe good vertuous workes true heed chryſte ☞ thou mayſte nat cone poynte withoute hys grace helpe well without grace thy workynge ſhalbe vnprofitable vayne lyke watcheth vayne beleueth kepe cytie without lorde therfore yf thou wylte fynde hys grace trewly ſolitarye two thynges neceſſarye vnto firſte thou ſo withdrawe thy ſelfe frō tranſitory thynges thou care yf none ſuche thou ſette thy ſelfe ſo vyle pryce thyne owne ſyght thou accompte thy ſelfe nought beleuynge men better thou arte pleaſe god ★ alſo ſo euer thou ſe relygyous perſones thynke good intente thoughe ſeme nat ſo mannes ſuſpition ofte deceyued therfore iuge thou nothynge certayne ſpeake nother thynge may ſounde thy owne prayſe laboure rather kepe thy vertue ſecrete thy vyces ☞ wyſe ſpeake yuell man howe trewe manyfeſte ſo euer gladely gyue herynge whan man prayſed whan diſprayſed alſo whan thou ſpekeſte let thy wordes trewe ſobre apte weighty god ſeculer man ſpeake aſke many queſtyons ſoone thou canſte breake tale ſet thoſe thynges god worldely thynge ſo euer happen howe dere beloued ſo euer vnto care god thynges ſuffred chryſte ſhorte wanne thereby euerlaſtynge ♣ thynke alſo aſwell tormentes goodman ioyes yuell men thys worlde paſte gone neuertheleſſe good men theyr tormentes haue receyued thus leſeſte hell wolde gyue worlde whan thou haſte tribulacions thynke heuen wante theym hell haue many mo euery daye leſt whan thou goeſt bed examyne diligently thou haſte thoughte day thou haſt ende thentent thou ſhalt diligently ymagine two cityes one full turmentes hell full cō ſolacyon kyngdome heuen behoueth neceſſyte entre come one beholde might draw againſt thy wyll vnto yuell cytye myght ſet good cytye trowe thou ſhalt fynde nothynge myght yf thou woldeſte thine herte turne god puttyng away neglygence wolde mekely call hym grace mercy whiche mooſte bleſſed aboue vouche ſafe birgettes reuelacyons l chapiter♣ mother god lady ſaynte mary ſpeketh ſpouſe ſonne ſaynt birget ſaienge thus nothynge ſo muche pleaſeth god man loue hym aboue thynge ſhall ſhewe ſymylytude pagan woman whiche knowynge nothynge faythe thoughe ſelfe thus knowe ſayde ſhe mater come thys worlde thynges came mother wombe ♣ beleue bene impoſſible ſhulde haue body ſo knyt togyther reaſon vnderſtandynge gyuen vnto therrfore knowe well ſome creatoure mayſter hathe made reaſonable creaure nat deformed lyke vnto wormes ſerpentes wherfore thynketh though many huſbandes called wolde rather come one callynge creatoure callynge haue alſo many ſonnes many doughters ne neuertheleſſe ſawe haue meate theyr handes knewe creatoure wante meate wolde take meate chyldren wolde gladly gyue vnto creatour haue alſo many poſſeſſyons whiche order myne owne wyll neuertheles yf knewe wyll creatour wolde gladely leaue myne owne wyll dyſpoſe honour doughter ſe god dyd thys pagan woman ſente vnto one electe ſeruauntes inſtructed faith god hym ſelfe viſyted herte thou mayſte well knowe vnderſtande hereafter anſwere woman ☞ whan man ſhewed vnto one god withoute begynnynge withoute endyng ſay creatoure maker thynges anſwered ſayde well beleued yt hath created thingꝭ hath creatour aboue hym lyke hys life euerlaſtynge myght gyue lyfe ★ whan woman herde ferther ſame creatoure toke manhoude vyrgyne preched worlde taught people owne perſone ſhe anſwered ♣ beleue god euery thynge ſhe ſayde ♣ pray ſhewe wordes creatoure dyd ſpeake commaunde wyll holly leaue myne owne wyll fully obey vnto hym euery worde hathe ſpoken whan declared vnto paſſyon lorde croſſe hys dethe hys reſurrecciō woman great wepyng anſwerered ſayde bleſſed creatour yt ſo pacyently ſheweth hys charite worlde v heuen therfore yf loued hym fyrſte bycauſe created nowe bounden loue hym bycauſe hathe ſhewed ſtreght waye vnto heuen hath redemed hys precyous blode bounde therfore ſerue hym ſtrength ye partes bodye bounden alſo remoue deſyre fyrſte poſſeſſyons chyldren kynſmen onely deſire ſe creatoure hys glorye neuer ſhall haue ende ſayde bleſſed lady ſaint birget lo doughter howe greate rewarde woman great loue ♣ dayly gyuen greate rewarde euery man loue hathe vnto god whyle lyueth thys worlde ❧our lorde ieſu chryſte gyueth ſpouſe ſaynte birget notable doctrine ye lyues actyue contēplatiue notable ſygnifyed martha mary magdaleyne ſaye howe man ſhall begyn profyte lyfe ſpūall grace vertue may finally aſcende vnto hyghe degre loue god hys neyghbour whiche doctryne appereth vi boke reuelacyons ſaynte birget lxv chapiter ſone god ſpeketh ſpouſe ſaynt birget ſayenge thus ★ two lyues whiche lykened martha mary magdaleyne ſo euer wyll folowe thoſe two lyues muſte make pure confeſſyon ſynnes takynge contricyon hauynge full wyl neuer offende fyrſte lyfe wytneſſe ſelfe goſpell mary magdaleyne dyd choſe whiche ledeth man contēplacion ſaye beholdinge heuenly thynges beſt parte way lyfe euerlaſtynge therfore euery man coueyteth folowe lyfe mary ſaye lyfe contemplatyue ſuffyſeth hym haue onely neceſſaryes body ſay clothynge without vanyte mete drynke ſcarſyte nat inſuꝑfluytye chaſtitie without yuell delectacyon faſtynge abſtynence ordynaunce churche faſteth muſte take hede nat ouermuche enfebled made weyke hys vnreaſonable faſtynge leſte thoroughe weyknes inforced leaue prayer counſayle gyuynge good dedes wherewith myghte bothe profyte hym ſelfe hys neyghboure alſo muſte alſo dilygently take hede nat hys faſtynge ye ſlowe iuſtice ſlaker workes mercy punyſhe rebel bryng infideles vnder yoke fayth requyſyte greate ſtrengthe well body ſoule ♣ therfore euery ſeke perſone wolde rather honour god faſte ete ſhall haue lyke rewarde hys good wyll faſteth charytie lyke wyſe obedyence eteth deſyring rather faſte thā eate ſhall haue lyke rewarde yt faſtethe seconde contemplatyue man ſhall nat ioye honoure worlde proſperyte thereof ne ſorowe aduerſyte ſhall ioye ſpecyally thys wycked men come deuoute men louers worlde come louers god good men profyte goodnes good labour dilygence ſeruyce god made dayly deuoute ☞ alſo contemplatyue man ſhall ſorowe ſynners made dayly worſe worſe almyghty god nat beloued hys creature ought commaundementes god diſpiſed ſette nought ★ thyrdely contemplatyue man may nat ydell ne maye vſeth actyue lyfe anone whan hath taken neceſſarye ſlepe ſhall ryſe thanke almyghty god herte hath create made thynges hys charyte takynge nature hathe reformed renewed mankynde ſhewynge hys paſſyon deathe loue hath man whiche ſo greate none greater ♣ alſo contemplatyue man ſhall thanke almyghty god theym ſaued purgatorye yet lyuynge worlde prayenge mekely vnto lorde ſuffre nat tempted aboue theyr power ☞ contemplatyue man alſo muſte dyſcrete hys prayer well ordered hys laudes prayſynges god yf haue ſufficyent lyue withoute laboure buſyneſſe muſte make longer prayer yf wery temptatyon ryſe hys prayer may laboure handes ſome honeſte profytable werke eyther hym ſelfe yf haue nede ☞ maner yrkeſome bothe ſaye prayer laboure may haue ſome honeſt occcupacion ſome good holſome wordes profytable counſeyls ſobernes ſcur • ylytie vncleane wordes ſette aparte tyll body ſoule made apte able ſeruyce god ★ contemplatyue man haue nat ſufficyent lyue labour maye make ſhorte prayer hys neceſſarye labour laboure ſhalbe perfeccion encreaſynge hys prayer nat laboure maye nat let nat hym aſhamed ne thynke nat greuous begge rather ioyous foloweth ſonne god made ſelfe poore make man ryche yf contemplatyue man vnder obedyence muſte lyue obedyence hys prelate hys rewarde ſhalbe double yf lybertye fourthly contemplatyue man maye nat couytous maye actyue man maye nat prodygall actyue man dyſtrybuteth temporall goodes god ſo contemplatyue man muſt diſtrybute hys ſpirytuall goodes morouer yf contemplatyue man wyll haue almyghty god inwardly herte let hym beware ſaye thus many ſuffyſeth yf ſaue myne owne ſoule yf ſo haue dedes men yf good ſelfe howe lyue doughter ſay think ſo ſawe theyr frende diſhoneſte troubled wolde renne theyr power deathe theyr frende myght delyuered trouble ſo ſhall contemplatyue man muſt ſorowe almyghty god offended hys brother whiche neyghbour hath occaſyon offende fall ſyn contemplatyue man ſhall endeuoure hym helpe hym oute ſynne diſcreſſyon yf haue trouble perſecucyon lette hym leaue place ſeke place quyet ſelfe good hym fyrſte houſe whiche geſtes maye ſlepe ſeconde clothynge clothe naked thyrde meate fede hungry fourth fyre warme theym colde ♣ fifte medicins ſeke ſaye good confortable wordes charyte god ❧★the god hys good dedes openly pryuely ſe maye glorifye god ♣ vnderſtāde contemplatyue man muſte put forthe two flame one ſecretely openly ſaye muſte haue double mekenes ☞ fyrſte muſte within forth herte ſeconde muſte without forth worlde firſte contemplatyue man thynke hym ſelfe vnworthy vnprofytable good warkes preferre nat hym ſelfe hys owne ſyght aboue man ne coueyte nat lauded ſene worlde flye pryde deſyre god aboue thynge folowing hys wordes teachinges contemplatyue man put forth ſuch flame good warkes hys herte ſhalbe illumyned charytye contrarious thynges come vnto hym ſhall lyghtly ſuffred ouercome ſeconde flame muſt openly perfyte mekenes herte muſte alſo appere hys apparell without forthe herde hys wordes performed hys dedes true mekeneſſe apparell whan contemplatyue man coueytet haue clothynge ſmal pryce whiche profitable clothyng greater value wherby maye fall pryde deſyre ſene worlde apparell lytell worth called ye worlde vyle abiecte fayre precyous god prouoketh mekenes apparrell greate pryce called fayre worlde foule vnſemely god takethe awaye fayrenes aungels ſaye mekeneſſe ☞ yf contemplatyue man reaſonable cauſe conſtrayned haue habyt ſomwhat better wolde let hym nat troubled therfore hys rewarde ſhall therby encreaſed alſo contēplatyue man muſte haue meakenes mouth ſaye ſpekynge meke thynges eſchewynge rybaldry ſuperfluytye wordes nat ſpeakynge ſubtylly ne diſceytfully ne preferrynge ſentence yf contemplatyue man hym ſelfe prayſed good dedes lette hym nat lyfte vp hys hert therfore anſwere thus laude honour god gyuech thynges ❧what duſte wynde goodnes commethe nought elles drye earthe withoute water ☞♣ yf reproued worlde lette hym nat moued therwith anſwere thus worthy thys muche haue ſo ofte offended god haue nat made amendes therfore agayne therfore praye ye therby ſuffring ſuche temporall reproues maye eſcape ſhames reproues euerlaſtynge ★ yf contemplatyue man prouoked anger wrathe vngoodly dealynge hys neyghbours lette hym well warre take good hede anſwere nat vndiſcretely cō menly pryde foloweth anger wrath therfore good coūſayle whan anger pryde come holde hys peace ſo longe tyme tyll wyll maye aſke helpe god ſuffre take good auyſemente howe anſwere maye fyrſte ouercome ſelfe wrathe ſhalbe abated herte ſo maye anſwere wyſely vnwyſe ☞♣thou ſhalte knowe alſo deuyll hath greate enuye contemplatyue man yf nat alway aſke helpe god hys wordes dedes gouerned hym holly directed vnto hym ♣ contemplatyue man muſte haue mekeneſſe workes ſay nothynge worldly prayſe ne attempte newe thynge hym ſelfe nat aſhamed worke vyle ſo euer ſo maye therby pleaſe god flye ſyngularytye good euery good dede dothe thynke myght haue better ♣ alſo muſte choſe ſytte rather poore men ryche rather obey thā commaunde kepe god take hede owne affeccyons alſo contemplatyue man muſte ofte vſe confeſſion ſtable dilygent temptacyons nat deſyre lyue none entente honoure god helthe ſoules maye encreaſed ★than contemplatyue man precious marchaundiſes whiche ſayde hys ſeruaunt ★ go ye ſhippe ſuche porte ther ſhall haue ryght greate encreaſe ye wynde ryſe laboure manfully yrke nat rewarde ſhalbe great ſeruaūt ſayled greate hearynge one mooſte faythfull ſeruauntes mooſte feruente ſorowynge throughe greate zele loue hys lorde toke vpon hym gouernaunce ſhyppe ſtrength brought ſhyppe porte lorde aſſigned go ☞is nat man ſo rewarde ★ fyrſte ſhall parte taker good dedes al bringeth ſafe port seconde glorie ſhalbe encreaſed without ende contrarywiſe ſhalbe come honoure prelacy theyr ambicyon ſhalbe parte taker paynes neyther contemplatyue mē actyue mē amende due penaunce ❧fyftly cōtemplatyue man muſte gyue medicyns gheſtes ſaye muſte conforte good wordes thynges come lykynge myſtykynge pleſaunt dyſpleaſaunt muſt ſaye thus wyll euery thynge pleaſeth lorde ſhulde wyll thoughe ſhulde go vnto hell ☞ truely ſuche wyll medicine thynges come vnto herte delyte trouble come greate temperaunce proſperyte ☞ bycauſe contemplatyue man hath many enemyes therfore muſte ofte make confeſſion longe wylfully abydeth ſynne hauyng tyme oportunytie confeſſed neglyente hedeth nat rather called apoſtata god contemplatyue man actyue lyfe ☞ alſo dedes man lyueth actyue lyfe thou ſhalte vnderſtande thoughe parte contemplatyue man beſt yet parte actyue man nat yuell laudable muche pleaſaunt god therfore ſhall ſhewe uowe howe actyue man muſte order hym ſelfe ★ muſte haue ye contemplatiue man hath fiue thinges firſt true faith holy church ſeconde knoweth commaundementes god coūſailes euangelycall truthe muſt performe wyll worde dede ♣thirdely muſte refrayne tonge yuell wordes agannſte god hys neyghbour hys handdes vnhoneſte vnlaufull dedes hys mynde ouermuch deſyre worldely goodes ouergreate delyte worldly pleaſures lerne contente god hath ſente hym deſyre ſuperfluous thynges fourthly ſhall dedes mercye reaſonably mekeneſſe ſo truſte tho good dedes nothynge offende god fyftly muſte loue god aboue thynges hym ſelfe martha dyd ſhe gaue ſelfe gladly folowynge wordes dedes afterwarde ſhe gaue goodes loue lothed temporall thynges deſyryng onely thynges euerlaſtynge therefore ſhe ſuſteyned thynges pacyently came cared well helth ſelfe thynkynge alwaye charitye poſſyon ſhe glad trouble mery aduerſities loued people mother chylde wolde alſo ofte folowe whan worlde deſyrynge nothynge alſo compaſſyon trouble ★ conforted theym heuyneſſe releued ſyke ſhe curſed man ne ſayde yuel man diſſymuled yuell maners neyghbours ſhe myght prayde alwaye ☞ therfore euery man deſyreth lyue charytabely actyue lyfe muſte folowe martha louynge neyghbour ende maye come heuen nat fauoure ſynne yuell lyfe flyenge hys owne prayſe pryde doubleneſſe hert wrath enuy may nat folowe thou ſhalte vnderſtande whan martha prayde brother lazar deed ſhe came fyrſte brother nat rayſed forwith vppon commynge afterwarde mary called whan ſhe came ye prayer togyther brother reyſed deathe ſpirytually deſyreth perfytely come lyfe contemplatyue muſt firſte exercyſe ſelfe well actyue lyfe labourynge maye honoure god good bodily labour lerne firſte reſyſte fleſſhly deſyres withſtande mightely fendes temptacyons maye afterwarde good delyberacyon aſcende hygher deg • e ſaye lyfe contemplatyue nat proued well aſſayed temptacyons hath nat yet fully ouercomme yuell mocyons fleſſhe maye nat holly ſette hym ſelfe heuenly thynges deed brother actyue man contemplatyue man vndiſcrete dedes many tymes good dede done vndiſcrete entent vnconſtaunt mynde therfore deed ★ wherfore good dede may acceptable god rayſed agayne commeth lyfe actiue man cōtemplatyue man ſaye whā neyghboure purely loued god god god onely deſyred ſelfe aboue thinges euery good dede man woman pleaſaūt god therfore ſaide goſpell mary choſen better parte ☞the lyfe actyue man good whan ſorowethe ſynnes neyghbours parte better whā laboureth maye hys neyghbours maye well perſeuer well vnto ende al dothe loue god part contemplatyue man beſte whan onely beholdeth heuenly thinges helth ſoules ♣ whan mynde fulfylled good affec • yons whan well reſte clamorous noyſe worldely buſyneſſe thynketh alwaye god preſente vnto hym ſetteth hys medytacyons fully loue god laboreth feruente fully therin daye alſo nyght ❧chriſte ſaythe deuocyon thinfideles tyme come ſhalbe much deuocyon chryſten men ſhall ſynge ioye father vnto ſonne holy gooſt honour al ſaintes amen vi boke reuelacions ſaynt byrgete lxxxiii chapiter ſonne god ſpeketh vnto hys ſpouſe ſaynte byrget ſainge thou ſhalte knowe yet ſhalbe ſo muche deuotyon infideles chriſten men ſhalbe theyr ſpirytuall ſeruauntes ſcrypture ſhalbe fulfylled ſaythe ☞ people nat vnderſtandynge ſhall gloryfye deſertes ſhalbe buylded agayne ſhal ioye vnto father ſonne holy ghoſte honour vnto sayntes amen ❧what thynges neceſſary hym deſyreth vyſyte landes infidel vi boke ye reuelacions saynte byrgette xl • chapiter ende ſayde chapiter ſonne god ſpeaketh ſaynt byrget ſaith deſyreth viſyte landes infidel ought haue v thynges firſte diſcharge hys conſcyence true confeſſyon contricion thoughe ſhulde forth dye seconde putte awaye al lyghtneſſe maners apparyll nat takynge hede newe cuſtomes vanytyes ſuche laudable cuſtomes aunceſters haue vſed tyme thyrdly haue temporall thynge neceſſytye honour god yf knowe thynge vnryghtwyſely gotten eyther hym ſelfe aunceſters reſtore whether lytel greate fourthly labour intente vnfaythfull men maye come true catholycall fayth nat deſyringe theyr goodes ne catell thing onely neceſſytye bodye ☞fyftely haue full wyll gladly dye honoure god ſo dyſpoſe hym ſelfe laudable conuerſacyon maye deſerue come good bleſſed endinge amen ¶finis
